Wuxi 74

North Wangting Bandits Seek Revenge: North Wangting Town, located at the junction of Suzhou and Wuxi, was suddenly attacked by sixty to seventy salt smugglers armed with rifles, box cannons, and other weapons at around 9 p.m. the night before last. Upon arriving at the town, they immediately opened fire as a show of force, surrounding the anti-smuggling team stationed inside the Yichang Cocoon Company from all sides and unleashing a barrage of gunfire. They looted extensively, stealing all the boxes, quilts, and other belongings of the anti-smuggling team members. They also burned a patrol boat and wounded a team member named Feng Youming. Upon hearing the alarm, Tan Shuren, the No. 2 patrol officer of the No. 6 team of the Second District of the water police stationed in the town, and Yang Songting, the No. 6 patrol officer, immediately led the police officers to suppress the bandits. After a fierce battle lasting half an hour, the bandits, unable to withstand the pressure, fled into Taihu Lake. It is said that the salt smugglers raided the town to avenge the deceased bandit leader Zhang Xiaoxiansheng. When the two sides exchanged fire, the smugglers shouted to the water police officers, "We are here specifically to make trouble for the anti-smuggling team and vent our past humiliation. This has nothing to do with you water police." The wounded team member Feng Youming was sent to the hospital for treatment yesterday.

The Tricycle Bureau Accused of Illegal Driving: The four steamship companies in this county, including Zhaoshang, Zhonghua, Xinshang, and Yonggu, recently accused the Yangxian Steamship Company of illegally operating steamships on the Zhangzhu line using a license belonging to the Jiangyin Yuxin Company, owned by Zhu Qian Shou. Yesterday, they specifically filed a petition with the county government, requesting a swift ban and requesting the ministry to revoke the license in order to uphold the law. Furthermore, the Xinan Public Steamship Bureau, which operates between Wuxi and Nanfangquan, accused the two steamship companies, Nandatongda, operating on the same route, of deliberately disobeying regulations. First, they disobeyed orders by adding late-night shifts, and then they arbitrarily lowered prices and solicited passengers everywhere, disrupting operations. Yesterday, the steamship bureau's representatives, Lu Shiquan and Wang Mingqing, jointly filed a petition with the county, requesting that the managers of the Nandatongda companies, Xiao Zhongquan and Yin Jianqing, be summoned and severely punished.

Theft Alarm at Dongba Bridge: In recent times, bandits have become so prevalent in the rural areas of Wuxi that they are almost everywhere. The family of Pu Ronglin, a resident of Dongba Bridge in the eastern part of Bashi Bridge in the Sixth District (Tianxia City), was suddenly attacked by five or six bandits at 3 a.m. the night before last. They broke into the house, first tying up and beating the entire Pu family, and then arbitrarily looting. They stole 100 yuan in banknotes and 50 silver dollars. After obtaining their loot, the bandits left with a shout. Yesterday morning, Jiang Jinhe, a farmhand of the Jiang family, spotted a bandit eating breakfast in a dim sum shop in Bashi Bridge Town. He immediately reported it to Gu, a special agent of the No. 1 team of the Second Squad of the town's police brigade, who led the police to capture him. Upon interrogation, the bandit confessed that his name was Wu Shigen, from Wu Lane in the Seventh District, and that he was 35 years old. He confessed to committing the crime at Ba Bridge last night and receiving seven silver dollars from the loot. According to the confession, Gu immediately escorted him to the county government for interrogation and handling.

Nantong 75

The Communist Bandits in the Eastern Countryside Can Be Expected to Be Eliminated: Communist bandits in the eastern rural areas of Nantong and Haimen counties have been colluding and causing disturbances. Recently, they were encircled and suppressed by the military and police, resulting in numerous captures and killings. The bandit's so-called 14th Red Army Corps has completely collapsed. Weapons and ammunition hidden in various places are being excavated as communist bandits who surrendered guide the authorities. More than 600 rifles have been recovered. On the 12th, Su Meijiang, a captured pseudo-brigade commander, was executed by firing squad. It is expected that they will be eliminated within half a month.

Large Numbers of Tenant Farmers in Coastal Reclamation Areas Are Kidnapped: The two gangs of sea bandits, Shen Guanxi and Zhou Xiangting, entrenched in the Heye River reclamation area of Sheyang, were defeated by the provincial security regiment. As the bandits dispersed, they kidnapped more than 80 tenant farmers from various districts in order to resist military pursuit and extort huge sums of money from various salt reclamation companies.

Various Circles Urge Exemption from Continuing to Send Wounded Soldiers: The Nantong 31st Rear Guard Hospital is already full of wounded soldiers. The Ministry of Military Affairs is planning to send a large number of wounded soldiers to Nantong. Various local circles, in addition to submitting a telegram requesting exemption, also sent representatives to Beijing to appeal for understanding of the actual difficulties in the local area and exemption from continuing to send more.

Conflict Between Water Police and Militia: A conflict occurred between the provincial water police team stationed in Qinglong Port and the 13th District militia. The team's headquarters was completely destroyed, and squad leader Zhong Jun and police officer Hu Songlin were injured. Both sides are currently in negotiations.

Zhenjiang 76

The Business Community Does Not Agree to Increase Telephone Fees: The Ministry of Communications previously ordered the Zhenjiang Telephone Bureau to increase prices by one yuan starting in September. The business community unanimously rejected this and repeatedly telegraphed the ministry, requesting that the original prices be maintained and the increase be postponed until the Zhenjiang telephone system was reformed. Recently, the Ministry of Communications ordered the Zhenjiang Bureau to insist on collecting the new increased price starting in September. The Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce convened a meeting of its executive committee to report the full text of the ministry's order. After discussion, it was decided to telegraph the ministry again, requesting consideration of the difficulties faced by businesses, and to send a circular to all trade associations and shops, instructing them to pay according to the original prices in accordance with the resolution. If anyone paid the new increased price before being notified to do so, they would be held responsible for the losses suffered by all the merchants in the town.

Changshu 78

Cui Shouzhi Buried in a Bandit's Den: The Deer River Town, located at the junction of Changshu and Taicang, was robbed by bandits last month, and Cui Shouzhi and eight others from the Yiheng Rice Shop were kidnapped, with a ransom of 180,000 silver dollars demanded. It is learned that the families were unable to pay the exorbitant ransom, so negotiations have been delayed for more than a month without reaching an agreement. It is now reported that Cui Shouzhi, who was kidnapped, was over 70 years old. On the night of the kidnapping, Cui was lying in bed wearing only a thin shirt and pants. The bandits seized him and dragged him away without allowing him to put on any clothes. He was dragged and pulled for several miles. Cui, being frail and old, was subjected to this cold and shock, and after arriving at the bandit's den, he fell ill and was unable to receive medical treatment, dying within a few days. The family was unaware of this. The other day, a private salt merchant arrived in town and reported to his family that Cui Shouzhi had died of illness. The Cui family was extremely alarmed and immediately sent someone to inquire. They met with the bandit leader and requested that the body be returned. However, the bandit leader said that there were many corpses here. If they wanted to see the body, they had to pay a viewing fee of ten silver dollars first. After identification, they would have to pay another 190 silver dollars (totaling 200 yuan) before they could take the body away. If they could not identify it, the viewing fee of ten yuan would be returned. The negotiator agreed and paid ten silver dollars. Then, he was led by several bandits to view the body. The body did not smell of decay, but the flesh was slightly withered. It was said that after each hostage died, they would be salted to preserve it for the family to claim. Now that it had been identified, the money could be paid to claim it. The negotiator returned to town and described what happened. Then, he took 190 silver dollars and went to claim the body, which was finally placed in a coffin and buried the day before yesterday. The remaining hostages have not yet been redeemed because the ransom has not been agreed upon, and they are still in danger.

Exposure of Fund-Raising Under False Pretenses: In the upper ten days of this month, someone calling himself Hu Guojun came to Changshu, acting quite extravagantly. After arriving in Changshu, he went to the county government to meet with County Magistrate Tan, carrying a letter from the Ministry of Interior, which stated that they were raising funds in various places for a blind, deaf, paralyzed, and disabled persons' home being established in the capital, due to a lack of funds. He requested protection from military and police along the way. At the time, County Magistrate Tan did not pay much attention and introduced him to the First District Office for assistance. He then raised 38 silver dollars. Hu then went to the Chamber of Commerce to meet with Chairman Xu Jingxi, intending to solicit donations from various businesses. Xu, suspicious of this sudden arrival and lack of official announcement, went to consult with the county magistrate, which aroused suspicion. That winter, he telegraphed the Ministry of Interior to inquire whether they had sent anyone to Changshu to raise funds. On the 13th, he received a reply stating that they had not sent anyone to Changshu and that there was no organization for a disabled persons' home in Beijing, indicating that it was a clear case of impersonation. The reply stated that they could be arrested and prosecuted. After receiving this letter, they searched everywhere for Hu Guojun, but he had disappeared without a trace.

Gaoyou 79

Incidents of Robbery Recorded Together: Shagou Town, under the jurisdiction of Yancheng County, was previously burned and looted by bandits, resulting in losses of more than 200,000 yuan. Less than two months later, on the early morning of the day before yesterday, more than 300 bandit ships carrying more than 2,000 bandits, each armed with guns, arrived again. After mooring, they went ashore one after another, searching and looting every household. They also burned down more than ten shops and more than twenty civilian houses. They abducted more than 100 men and women as hostages and shot several townspeople. They did not leave Shagou until the next morning, entrenching themselves in Wangjia Village nearby. After receiving the news, County Magistrate Wang of this county ordered Police Brigade Commander Mu Shi Du to lead a team to join forces with the military and police of Yantai and Baoying counties to encircle and suppress the bandits. Furthermore, in Xinsha, the Sixth District of the county, more than ten bandits suddenly arrived at around 8 p.m. the night before last, each armed with guns, and searched and looted every household, with no one spared. It is said that the losses were enormous. Furthermore, Quan Yuliang, a wealthy resident of Shaguan Village in the county, was kidnapped by bandits previously. Due to the exorbitant ransom demanded, he has not yet been redeemed. The night before last, more than ten bandits arrived again, each armed with guns, and broke open the main gate of the Quan family. They entered and looted everything, and they also captured Quan Yuliang's cousin, Quan Yu Bao, instructing him to quickly prepare 50,000 yuan to redeem Quan Yuliang. After Yu Bao's repeated negotiations, it was agreed that they would pay 2,700 yuan before the bandits left with a shout.

Dingyuan 80

Local Groups Oppose the New County Magistrate: The Dingyuan County Chamber of Commerce, Finance Management Office, Education Bureau, and district chiefs of all twenty districts in the county, Zhou Huantong, and others, telegraphed the chairman and civil affairs director of the Anqing Provincial Government, stating that since County Magistrate Xu took office in Dingyuan, he had worked diligently to govern the county, eliminated violence, and brought peace to the people, who relied on him for tranquility. They later heard that the provincial government had issued an order to appoint Li Wanshi as acting county magistrate of Dingyuan. They were just about to telegraph to request that the order be withdrawn when rumors spread that there was news of Fang Shaozhou being appointed instead. Upon hearing this, they were deeply fearful. It was discovered that in the autumn of 1927, Fang Shaozhou, using the name of the 33rd Army's Special Operations Team, entrenched himself within the county seat and surrounding areas, kidnapping people from every household, extorting police firearms, seizing educational land and public funds, and extorting more than 100,000 yuan. His actions were similar to those of bandits. They implored the provincial government to consider the people's concerns and immediately withdraw the order, preventing Fang from coming to Dingyuan, and also to telegraph County Magistrate Xu, instructing him to remain in his post with peace of mind in order to maintain local stability.

Taizhou 81

Robbery Case Occurred at Jiangxia Desert: At Zhou Zuomei's house in Jiangxia Desert, located about five li outside the city of Linhai Xiamen, more than ten bandits suddenly arrived in the middle of the night, broke down the door, and threatened them with guns. They stole jewelry, clothes, quilts, and other items worth more than 400 silver dollars, and kidnapped Zuomei's brother, Xu Da, and nephew, Yongxiang.

Wuyuan 82

Banditry Rampant in Wuyuan's Border Areas: Wuyuan County is located near the Jiangxi border, and banditry has been rampant recently. Unemployed coal miners from Hubei and Jiangxi, as well as local bandits from Lede, are also constantly stirring up trouble. The other day, bandits from Leping invaded Kengtou, a village in the northern part of the county, and looted extensively. All 300 households in the village were affected, with losses estimated at more than 30,000 yuan. Yesterday afternoon, more than twenty kiln workers from nearby Yaopeng, armed with knives and guns, went to Shuanglukou, a village in the northern part of the county, to rob. Fortunately, the area was close to the two large villages of Fengshan and Hongguan, and the bandits, being few in number, did not dare to invade other villages. They only went to Defeng Fabric Shop and looted more than 1,000 yuan. At the time, Fengshan heard the alarm and quickly summoned hunters to track and pursue the bandits. Four bandit leaders were captured and have been sent to the county government today for investigation.

Local News

The Ministry of Education Approves the Methods for the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau's Academic Competition for Middle Schools 86

The Ministry of Education, based on the sixteen articles of the academic competition methods for middle schools submitted by Chen Dezheng, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, instructed: "The submitted documents have been read in detail. After reviewing the sixteen articles of the methods, they are generally suitable and approved for filing. However, articles 11 and 15 both contain the phrase 'this committee,' so the name of this method should add the word 'committee' after the word 'competition.' Please comply with this instruction." The methods are recorded below:

▲Methods for the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau's Academic Competition Committee for Middle Schools: (1) In order to arouse the interest of young people in studying academic subjects, the Bureau will hold various academic competitions for middle schools. (2) Various academic competitions will be divided into junior high and senior high (including vocational schools) divisions and will be held in groups according to the subjects offered by each school. (3) All municipal and registered private middle schools in the city must participate in various academic competitions. (4) Private middle schools in the city that are not registered and wish to participate in various academic competitions must submit an application to the Bureau for approval two weeks before the competition. (5) Various academic competitions are divided into representative competitions and free competitions. (6) In representative competitions, all students in the school will first hold preliminary competitions to select representatives to participate in the competition. The method for selecting representatives will be determined by each school and reported to the Bureau. (7) In free competitions, individuals will be the unit, and each school will report to the Bureau to participate in the competition. (8) The scope or questions of the subjects for each competition will be determined by the Bureau. (9) The preliminary, semi-final, or final competitions for various academic competitions will be determined according to the nature of the subject. (10) At least one competition will be held for each of the junior high and senior high divisions each academic year. The subjects, times, locations, and grouping methods of the competitions will be determined by the Bureau on an ad hoc basis. (11) Judges will be hired by this committee, and the judging criteria will be determined separately by the Bureau according to the nature of the subject. (12) Those with excellent competition results will be specially awarded certificates of commendation or prizes by the Bureau. (13) Awards will be divided into individual awards and school awards, with the top five being awarded. If there are a large number of participants, the number of winners may be increased as appropriate. (14) Those who rank first in the competition will not be allowed to participate in the same subject in the same division in future competitions. (15) The expenses of this committee will be allocated by the Bureau. If there is a need for experimental equipment and consumables, it will be provided by each school. (16) These methods will be implemented from the date of approval by the Municipal Government.

The Dawn of the Future of Jinan University 87

▲President Zheng is willing to overcome difficulties during the celebration

▲To create the highest overseas Chinese institution of the Three People's Principles

Overseas Chinese students from various provinces and cities at the National Jinan University held a meeting at Zhiyuan Hall at the school yesterday afternoon at 1:30 p.m. to celebrate Zheng Hongnian's appointment as the full-time president of the school. More than 1,000 people attended. The Jinan University Alumni Association in the capital and Shanghai sent representatives to congratulate him. The venue was decorated with a large banner celebrating Zheng's appointment, making it a grand occasion. The ceremony was performed as usual. First, Chairman Fu Ruiwu delivered the opening speech, stating that President Zheng bears the responsibility of creating and completing the school. This time, he resigned from industrial and political affairs, purely based on his original aspiration 23 years ago and his enthusiasm for caring for overseas Chinese children. Today, students from various provinces and cities are holding this grand meeting. In addition to their inner gratitude, they hope that President Zheng will continue to develop the school with his spirit of enduring hardship. Kang Laiwen and Wang Weiyin, representatives of the Jinan University Alumni Association in the capital and Shanghai, successively delivered congratulatory speeches. Mr. Zheng stood up and said that he was very gratified that everyone had come to celebrate his appointment as president. Since leaving the school, he had been in politics for many years and believed that all social undertakings must start with education. He felt that he had made no contribution to transportation in the past. All contributions were in education. In the ninth year of the Republic, he started vocational education on the railway, planting the seeds of labor education. He only sought to be beneficial to society and the country and to have a clear conscience, without liking publicity or seeking recognition. He maintained a skeptical attitude everywhere and studied with an open mind. "Overseas Chinese education" was created by him, and at first, it was not noticed by others. Because education should be done for education's sake, it should not be used for political activities, and young people should not be used as tools. This is the purpose of his education. He has said this repeatedly since he became the principal of this school. He is willing to be an educator for life. He is grateful for everyone's celebration and hopes that he can fully develop as the president. No matter how difficult it is in the future, he will continue to enrich the content and actively expand. He only hopes that the students will understand the purpose of his overseas Chinese education, which is to restore the national spirit, to repay the overseas Chinese for their contribution to the revolution, and to educate their children for the prime minister to thank the overseas Chinese elders. Therefore, he hopes that everyone will implement the Prime Minister's instructions, believe in the Three People's Principles. He personally does not need to be supported, what he wants to support is the Prime Minister's instructions, the Three People's Principles. Therefore, he hopes that everyone will work together to complete the highest overseas Chinese institution of the Three People's Principles. Then, Vice President Hong Qiling said that President Zheng is like a loving mother, and everyone is a good child. He is one of the nannies and hopes to keep today's deep impression forever. His words were very humorous and sincere. Then, Xu Kecheng talked about the indelible glorious history of overseas Chinese supporting the revolution. Then, the Western orchestra played several songs and served refreshments, ending with joy. Furthermore, the school held a school affairs meeting at Huaan Building at 4:00 p.m. yesterday, passing many important cases for improvement, which did not end until late at night.

Japanese Residents in Shanghai Establish a Secondary Commercial School 90

Japanese residents in Shanghai discussed establishing a secondary school for boys in Shanghai in May. On the 13th of this month, the residents' meeting proposed the establishment of a commercial school. After discussion by the Japanese residents present, it was unanimously approved. However, due to the fact that economic and school building matters could not be prepared at one time, it was decided to postpone the opening of the school until April next year. The school will be located in the Japanese Higher Elementary School on North Sichuan Road. It is reported that the school will have a five-year course, and the curriculum will take into account both employment in business and further education after graduation. The budget is estimated at 17,640 yuan for the first year, 25,150 yuan for the second year, 33,890 yuan for the third year, 43,680 yuan for the fourth year, and 53,580 yuan for the fifth year. Each class will enroll 40 students, and preferential treatment will be given to children of Japanese residents in Shanghai.

Literary Figure Sheng Cheng Returns Home 94

Sheng Cheng, a native of Yizheng, Jiangsu, went to Europe in the eighth year of the Republic under a work-study program. He graduated from the Royal Silk Academy of Badua in Italy and entered the Advanced National Agricultural Sericulture Department of Montpelier in France, obtaining a master's degree in advanced science. He then served as a lecturer in comparative sericulture at the University of Paris. Although Mr. Sheng studied science, he had a special passion for literature. His French works such as "My Mother," "My Mr. Sheng," "Mother and I," "Autumn Heart Beauty," and "Ten Years of Wandering" are all well-known in European literary circles. In particular, "My Mother" has been widely circulated and translated into English, Spanish, German, and Dutch. Last year, he traveled extensively to countries in the Near East, such as Turkey, Greece, Egypt, Palestine, Syria, and India. He arrived in Shanghai by ship from Bombay the day before yesterday. Due to the death of his grandmother, he must first return home before coming back to Shanghai to publish his works from the past ten years.

Chi Chih Basketball Team Defeats Tongji 96

▲ Result: 29 to 14

The Chi Chih and Tongji University basketball teams played a friendly match at the China Basketball Hall at 7:15 PM last night. Chi Chih won with a score of 29 to 14. The referee was Qu Hongren. The performance of both teams was not very impressive, probably due to their unfamiliarity with the techniques and disorganized formations. The score in the first half was quite close. Tongji scored first with one point. Then, Chi Chih had four or five free throw opportunities, but none of them were successful. After a long period of competition, Tongji added two more points, winning with a score of 3 to 0. From then on, Chi Chih's spirit suddenly rose, and their score increased steadily, while Tongji fell behind. At the end of the first half, Chi Chih had ten points and Tongji had eight points.

Starting in the second half, Tongji's fighting spirit slightly declined, while Chi Chih continued to fight hard. Yang Yulin and Wei Haiqing scored repeatedly, and the score jumped to 25 to 20. Tongji was difficult to move under Chi Chih's close supervision. As a result of the match, Chi Chih won with a score of 29 to 14.

Protest Against the Xingguang vs. Baota Match 99

According to news from the Xingguang Sports Association, the Xingguang football team played against Baota in the first division championship at the China Baseball Field last week. The match was originally scheduled to start at 3:00 PM, but the referee had not arrived by 3:15 PM. The captain of the Xingguang team inquired with Zhou Jiaqi of the Progressive Association, who said that he had not received any notice from the Westerners. Therefore, the Progressive Association appointed Shen Huichun as the referee, and the match started at 3:20 PM. In the first half, both sides played tight offense and defense, and neither scored. After the break, the match continued. After about 38 minutes of play, the referee blew his whistle and said that a Xingguang player had committed a foul and awarded a penalty kick. Fortunately, the goalkeeper caught the ball and kicked it out. Not a minute later, a Baota player committed the same foul, and the referee also awarded a penalty kick. Unexpectedly, the Baota linesman made rude remarks, entered the field to interfere, and resisted the referee, not allowing the penalty kick to be taken. After the referee warned him, he finally retreated, but he was still not convinced. In the last five minutes, the linesman took the opportunity to wave the flag arbitrarily. The referee immediately asked him why, and the linesman said that the Xingguang goalkeeper had taken seven steps, forcing the referee to award a free kick, resulting in a score of 1 to 1. However, Xingguang's morale was greatly affected by the unwarranted accusation, and the players were unwilling to attack or defend. In the last two minutes, they lost the game. The Xingguang Sports Association believes that the Baota linesman arbitrarily disrupted the game and caused the referee to be unable to perform his duties, so the result should not be considered valid. It is said that they have filed a protest with the Westerners Association yesterday.

Chinese Women's Sports 100

By Chen Zhang'e, Director of the Physical Education Department of Jinan University (1)

The author has lived in Southeast Asia for a long time and is not familiar with the sports situation in China. In addition, my knowledge is limited, so I dare not discuss sports. Now, in response to the invitation of the Shenbao editor, I will simply raise a question, and this question is "Chinese Women's Sports." This issue of Chinese women's sports was also promoted many times during my lectures in Guangzhou last summer, but there was no complete publication. Now I can tell you everything. Everyone knows that women's sports is an important issue. In the past, we didn't understand or talk about sports at all, which led to China's decline. Now it's better. You see, in recent years, whether it is schools, groups, or families, they all pay attention to sports. However, no one in the women's sector has come out to promote it, which is a kind of regret. We know that there are 400 million people in China, half men and half women. Among them, 200 million are men, and 200 million are women. Men should pay attention to sports, and women should pay even more attention. They should pay more attention than men, because today's women are the mothers of the country in the future. If today's women are not healthy, their bodies will not be strong when they grow up in the future. Then the little citizens they pass down in the future will also become weak. It can be seen that today's women have a great relationship with the strength of our nation. Now, let's first discuss a small question with all the readers. This is something that is necessary for life. What do you think this is? This is something that we cannot leave for a moment, and that is air. If we don't have air in a few minutes, we cannot live. If we don't have water or rice, we will die in seven or eight days or dozens of days. If we don't have sunlight or if we work all day long without a moment's rest, we will not be able to survive for a long time. However, if we have all of the above needs, can we live? I'm afraid we still can't. For example, if there is a person now, we give him fresh air and plenty of sunlight every day, and we also give him plenty of food and drink, and we also tell him to rest every day, don't let him run, and don't let him walk. Just sit still all day long. What do you think will happen to this person? We can be sure that he will die in three or four months. Everyone can understand this point, so we can know that exercise is a very important thing in life. You see, when people are first born, they fall to the ground with a "gua gua" sound, waving their hands and kicking their feet. This is the first exercise in life. The term exercise can also be called physical education. Now I want to talk about the importance of physical education and its meaning. Modern educators all acknowledge that it (physical education) is an important science in education and the foundation for creating a complete personality. All readers should know that physical education is the most important of all educations. Physical education is the foundation for creating a personality. What does it mean to be the foundation of a personality? For example, if we want to build a building, the construction of this building should have five major elements. The first point is magnificence. It must be able to make everyone praise it. It must be magnificent and grand, so if our building is magnificent, people will unanimously praise it. The second is layout. Our building is able to achieve the purpose of magnificence because the host has artistic knowledge and careful research. The third is planning. Planning is extremely important. Before we build a building, we must first have engineers discuss the specific plan before it meets the principles of architecture. The fourth is raw materials. If our building has a specific plan, the layout is neat, and the appearance is magnificent, but the raw materials are not good, the wood is old, the iron is rusty, and the bricks, stones, sand, and soil are not strong, the house built in this way will not last long. Therefore, raw materials are also an element of construction. The fifth is the foundation. This issue is very important. If the elements of this building are good, the planning, layout, and magnificence are all pleasing, but the foundation is not good or it is built on loose sand or on a sandy slope, wouldn't it be very dangerous once the wind rises and the tide comes? Therefore, a solid foundation is the most important issue in building a building. We want to cultivate children so that they become healthy people, and it is almost the same as this construction method. (To be continued)

▲ Should strive to develop construction projects hereafter

Shanghai Mayor Zhang Qun, who was previously ordered by the Central Government to go to Liaoning for negotiations, arrived in Shanghai yesterday afternoon at 2:30 PM after being away for three months. Mr. Zhang, accompanied by Fang Benren, the Central Government representative stationed in Liaoning, arrived by the Dalian Maru and disembarked at the Huangpu Wharf. Prior to this, the Garrison Headquarters and the Public Security Bureau's Detective Team had provided strict security around the wharf. Those who went to welcome him were very enthusiastic, including Yu Hongjun, Yin Rugeng, Liu Jiwen, and Xiong Shihui's representative Chen Yuxiang, Yuan Ludeng, Yan Shenyu, the Municipal Party Headquarters' Zhu Yingpeng, Fan Zhengbo, the Public Security Bureau Chief Yuan Liang, as well as the chiefs of various bureaus, counselors, section chiefs, and captains of the water patrol teams, totaling no less than a hundred people. At that time, it was raining heavily, and all the welcomers stood in the rain, complaining incessantly. Fortunately, after the Dalian Maru docked at the wharf, the rain eased slightly. Mr. Zhang disembarked first and greeted everyone individually. Fang Benren then also disembarked, and they all returned to their residences by car to rest.

▲ Planned Steps After disembarking, Mr. Zhang was approached by our newspaper reporter for an interview. Mr. Zhang first stated, "My trip to Liaoning was originally scheduled for three weeks, but unexpectedly, I stayed in Liaoning for as long as three months. The security of Shanghai City relies on the maintenance of Commander Xiong and the comrades of the Party Headquarters, as well as all sectors of society. It remains peaceful as always. This should be specially stated and thanked first. Furthermore, this time, Deputy Commander Zhang's telegram to send troops to take office, the manifestation of past facts, and the future measures have all been closely negotiated with the Central Government in advance. This is a kind of planned step. The rumors outside are absolutely unbelievable. It is even said that Deputy Commander Zhang has other views on the party and government, which is not worth a smile from those in the know. Deputy Commander Zhang extremely agrees with what Chairman Chiang Kai-shek said in his telegram: all subsequent dispositions will be completely in accordance with the Central Government. This should be stated second."

▲ Source of Rumors Mr. Zhang also said, "The source of rumors is Dalian and Tianjin in the north, and Shanghai and Hong Kong in the south. Shanghai is especially a concentrated area for various rumors. The public should pay special attention to it and not believe it lightly. After the national general mobilization, Yan and Feng have been defeated. The second step is the national general mobilization to work hard on construction projects. The responsibility for construction should be jointly borne by the government and the people. If we only blame the government, it is like planting trees: the government cultivates them, and the people discard them, then planting is the same as not planting. For example, the floods in western Liaoning were due to the efforts of all sectors of society in Shanghai to raise relief funds. The Northeast authorities are extremely grateful, and they attribute the cause of the floods in western Liaoning to the public's inability to properly manage the rivers, often padding the banks with soil to reduce the riverbed and increase planting, so that the rivers gradually narrowed. Once the water rises, it is inevitable that it will flood. Therefore, although the government dredges the rivers and diverts water, the public must also protect them well."

▲ Firmly Declines Concurrent Position Mr. Zhang expressed his firm refusal to take the position of Chairman of the China Merchants Bureau Reorganization Committee. He said, "With my personal talents, I already feel overwhelmed to take charge of Shanghai's municipal administration. Moreover, I have been running around for national affairs and have no time to spare. In this year alone, I have gone to Fujian and Liaoning in ten months, which has taken up half of my time. After this, I should urgently work hard to make up for the previous losses. How can I have the spare time to take care of other things? I hope my humble sincerity can be understood."

▲ Chiang-Zhang Meeting When asked if Deputy Commander Zhang plans to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek recently, he replied, "It has not been decided recently, but Zhang said before I left that he should come to Nanjing often in the future. Wu Tiecheng has gone to Tianjin to preside over the oath-taking ceremony for Wang Shuchang and Yu Xuezhong. Wang Jinyu will stay in Liaoning to negotiate. When Wu returns to his domain, Wang will go south. Deputy Commander Zhang recently expressed his opinion that the most important thing at present is to quell the chaos. After the chaos is quelled, he will devote all his efforts to construction. His true intentions can be seen in this." It is said that Mr. Zhang and Mr. Fang are scheduled to go to Nanjing today to meet with Chiang Kai-shek and report everything.

Large Batch of Japanese Sample Rice 103

▲ Arrived yesterday on a Japanese ship

▲ Rice industry announces boycott

According to Guowen News Agency, the Japanese government has commissioned Mitsui & Co. to ship a large batch of Japanese rice to Shanghai for sale, which has become a fact. According to reliable information yesterday, the first batch of sample rice has already been shipped by Mitsui's Wakayama Maru and arrived in Japan yesterday morning. After import, it was berthed at Mitsui Wharf in Pudong. The total number of imports is estimated to be 18,300 stones. Although the Municipal Government's Social Bureau and other departments have paid attention to this matter, the central government has not yet issued an order to investigate and prohibit it, so it is too late to prohibit its import. The ship originally planned to import it in Hong Kong, but after learning that the customs had not yet taken action, it was shipped directly to Shanghai. The second batch is even larger and is planned to be shipped to Shanghai as quickly as possible before the prohibition order is issued. The planned number of 100,000 stones will be shipped in four batches. In addition, more than 100,000 stones have been shipped to Southeast Asia.

Sun Zhentong respectfully informs rice merchants to boycott the shipment of Japanese rice to Shanghai for sale, saying, "The source of the revolution is due to the economic aggression of the great powers, which is becoming increasingly serious. The ancestral country is seeing its demise. The late Prime Minister said in his lectures on the Principle of People's Livelihood that China is a country established on agriculture, and food is the most important thing for the people. The entire life of farmers and citizens is the center of society, which has the ability to support the prosperity of urban economy and politics. The Prime Minister's last words still say that the evil forces have not been exhausted, and the aggression has not stopped. He exhorted future generations to continue to work hard to resist aggression in order to save the country from danger. Unexpectedly, in the eight years since then, only Saigon and Min Dang foreign rice were imported into China at first. In the most recent four years, there have been large and small shipments of wrapped rice. This year, there has been an increase in Burmese Kegan rice coming to China. How can our country bear the loss of foreign rice? I remember that a few years ago, more than a hundred rice merchants went bankrupt because of this, and their vitality was greatly lost. Japan, a country established on industry, can fill China with millions of agricultural products, silk cotton clothing materials, etc. In the past, Zhentong also found it difficult to describe them in detail. Now I see Japan shipping a large number of agricultural products, silk cotton, and cloth, which is fatal to our country's silk cotton and cloth merchants. In Shanghai and Wuxi alone, hundreds of silk factories and thousands of cloth factories have been closed, and hundreds of thousands of unemployed men and women workers are waiting to die with no way to maintain themselves. It is really heartbreaking to talk about this. I am saddened by the fact that unscrupulous merchants are greedy for huge profits, acting as accomplices and harming the country and the people. The dangerous situation is so great that it could erupt at any moment. Are my rice merchants aware of this? On October 10th, various newspapers reported that Japan was shipping millions of stones of toxic rice from stockpiles to China for trade, and the first batch will arrive in Shanghai. They are heavily bribing unscrupulous merchants and entrusting them with sales. Compatriots, this is not just the outflow of rights, but it is actually handing over a knife to kill people. The previous aggression was only against silk cotton cloth merchants and coolie workers, but now it is not only frustrating rice merchants, but also affecting tens of millions of farmers. Foreign insults are coming one after another, so that food and clothing are also controlled by others. After a few years, destruction can be expected. Those who have a little conscience are all terrified. Alas, my people, if we continue to endure without resisting, what consequences can we imagine? I hope that the wise men in charge will plan for mediation, strictly prohibit imports, and save a glimmer of hope. Zhentong cries out to my beloved rice merchant giants and patriotic gentlemen: Even if the Japanese in China do not eat Chinese rice, they must not be blinded by greed and lose all conscience, willingly acting as killing machines. I hope that the people of the country would rather starve to death than eat Japanese rice. I also hope that other foreign rice will be completely eliminated from our country as soon as possible. It is a matter of life and death, and you must not underestimate it. Industry and agricultural products are all under control. The rise and fall of the country is the responsibility of everyone. Step by step, the danger is coming closer and closer. What I mean is dangerous, so I am giving you my sincere advice. I hope you will consider it carefully."

The Nature of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Will Be Determined at the Fourth Plenary Session 109

▲ Song Shuqiao Reported at the Memorial Week Ceremony

Since the National Government announced the appointment of Li Zhonggong as the Chairman and General Manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, the various initiatives have been full of vitality and have been highly valued by all parties. Recently, during the autumn festival according to the lunar calendar, many considered it a difficult time. Mr. Li has calmly dealt with it. The remaining scattered debts are also being repaid gradually. In terms of personnel, he focuses on employing people based on their talents. In terms of finance, he strives to increase revenue and reduce expenditure. The issue of the nature of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has always been a central point of contention. On National Day, Mr. Li drafted an article entitled "Fundamental Issues in Reorganizing the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company," which also expressed a very clear position. Mr. Li went to Nanjing the day before yesterday. It is said that he will present to the National Government and Chairman Chiang on the recent situation and fundamental issues of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and also intends to propose a fundamental reform plan. Also, at the Memorial Week ceremony the day before yesterday, the Secretary-General of the Bureau, Song Shuqiao, reported on behalf of the chairman, also explaining the nature of the Bureau. The general idea was that with the Fourth Plenary Session about to convene, the National Government's political construction would better satisfy the demands of the general public. Regarding the Bureau, in my opinion, the main reason for the decline of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company lies in "illness" rather than "poverty." The reason why the Bureau is poor is due to many malpractices. Saving the poor without eliminating the malpractices will not change its poverty. If the accumulated malpractices can be eliminated, it is not difficult to reorganize the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, which has assets worth 40 million and debts of only 13 million. However, since the fundamental nature has not yet been determined, there are bound to be some difficulties. This time, General Manager Li went to Nanjing to report on the work progress and will also present to the National Government and Chairman Chiang on the nature of the Bureau, and intends to request the Fourth Central Plenary Session to discuss and resolve the matter decisively. As for the Bureau's appointment, dismissal, and treatment of staff, and its security system, it has never been perfect. In the future reorganization, we should follow the established rules of the Post Office, and adopt examination methods or other screening methods for employing people, and select true talents with a fixed legal system. For positions, we should find ways to ensure their stability, so that they can stay in their positions for a long time and perform their duties and abide by the law. Regarding remuneration, the principle of "generous salary to foster integrity" should be applied so that they can maintain their livelihood and not have the bad habit of taking improper gains. However, what needs to be noted is that the method must be strict; otherwise, if the salary is already generous but integrity is not fostered, then the Bureau staff will serve the public, not individuals, and will not panic because of changes in the head of the department. Further, the heads of such transportation agencies have administrative nature and are not purely political in nature, and their term of office should also be longer. The term of office of the President of Nippon Yusen Kaisha was also declared to be 15 years at the beginning of the government's trusteeship. In the future, if the nature of the Bureau can be decisively determined as state-owned, this system of protecting service personnel can be adopted, and the future will not be difficult to usher in a new era.

Foreigners Arbitrarily Laying Telephone and Water Lines 110

▲ Ministry of Communications Informs the Municipal Government to Order a Cease

The Ministry of Communications, based on Article 4 of the contract signed between the Shanghai Telephone Bureau and the China Foreign Company in the 14th year of the Republic of China, limited the water line to Pudong to a maximum of 75 pairs of core wires. Now, the company has arbitrarily laid new water lines, increasing to 150 pairs of core wires. It is difficult to guarantee that there are no other purposes. In addition to ordering the Shanghai Telephone Bureau to first prohibit the use of the extra 75 pairs of core wires in the laid water lines, it is also responsible for ordering the company to repair the old water lines or add a new water line with 75 pairs of core wires, and dismantle the currently laid 150 pairs of core wires to comply with the original plan. It also sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Government, instructing the water and land public security agencies that if foreigners lay water and land electric lines in the Chinese concession in the future without the approval of the Ministry and notification on record, they should be strictly prohibited to prevent encroachment.

Special Circumstances in the Bean and Rice Industry 114

▲ Request to Modify the Year-End Account Settlement Date According to the National Calendar

Ye Huijun, a standing committee member of the Shanghai Bean and Rice Industry Association, submitted a document to the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau, stating that it was a request to temporarily modify the account settlement with merchants according to the national calendar. He respectfully presented his views and requested instructions. Since the Republic of China, the solar calendar has been adopted, and merchants' accounts are settled at the end of May, the end of September, and the end of December, in three phases. The end of May is 26 days later than the 5th day of the 5th lunar month, and the end of September is one and a half months later than the 15th day of the 8th lunar month. Therefore, comparing the new and old calendars, there is no difference between the Dragon Boat Festival and the Mid-Autumn Festival of the abolished lunar calendar. However, judging from the past experiences, various difficulties have already been felt. If the end of December is used, this year it will be the 12th day of the 11th lunar month, which cannot be postponed. It is about 50 days earlier than the abolished lunar calendar. During this transition period, it is extremely difficult, especially for our rice industry. Now, I will explain the commercial habits of our bean and rice industries to you, Sir. The transactions of the bean and rice industries, apart from cash transactions, have two types of account settlement: large and small month-end settlements and three-festival settlements. In this street, the scattered households and rural customers mostly settle their accounts at the three festivals. They cannot pay off the debts at the end of May and the end of September, and the year-end is often the time for total settlement. This has been a long-standing practice and has become an unchangeable fact. There are no less than 110 bean and rice companies in Shanghai, with monthly transactions of no less than seven or eight million yuan. Usually, funds are used for circulation, and they are collectively closed at the end of the period. Since the promulgation of the clear order to change to settling accounts according to the solar calendar, banks and money shops will inevitably urge for payment when the deadline arrives. However, our country is an agricultural country, and the harvest of agricultural products must be until mid to late November. Taking rice as an example, from doing rice (commonly known as "throwing rice") to drying rice, to grinding rice, to transporting and selling it in rural and urban areas, to reselling it in commercial ports, all kinds of procedures cannot be completed in one or two months. Our industry can start accumulating stocks between December and January of the solar calendar. If we settle accounts at the end of the solar calendar, when we need funds to purchase goods, we have to settle accounts with financial institutions. Funds are stagnant and cannot circulate, and commerce will stagnate. Our industry's annual plan lies in the winter. If we do not accumulate stocks at this time, we will have no goods to supply the market in the coming year. This is the first reason why it is not possible. Farmers rely on selling goods to get money, and they get money to repay debts. Rural stores also rely on the return of debts to settle their accounts. Our industry receives this account and then settles it with the silver and money industry. This has been a practice for thousands of years and cannot be changed due to seasonal restrictions. If we settle accounts at the end of the year, our industry will not be able to accumulate rice stocks. Rice merchants and farmers will not be able to obtain funds. Finance is like a tide, flowing from the sea to the river to the port and the ditch. If one way is blocked, hundreds of streams will not flow. Low grain prices are already hurting farmers, and grain stagnation will make farmers unable to survive. This is the second reason why it is not possible. Based on these two reasons, settling accounts at the end of the year actually has many difficulties. Therefore, the money industry associations of Nanjing, Suzhou, Wuxi, Wujin, and Danyang counties recently proposed to set the end of January each year as the closing date, which suggests a fiscal year. At the beginning of this year's preparations, the lower half of the month should be temporarily moved, that is, February 15 of the 20th year as the final closing date. The association believes that the situation of our rice industry is more special than other industries. As mentioned above, it is practically difficult to settle accounts at the end of the year. It is inevitable to request another method and make a special modification. Some may say that correcting the calendar is an important task for establishing a country, as recorded in historical records. Why should we be perfunctory? Moreover, is our country the only country in the world that is based on agriculture? They follow the solar calendar, and we have not heard of any difficulties. Why should we be so argumentative? The answer is that correcting the calendar is one thing, and settling accounts for merchants is another. The fiscal year may adopt March, July, or other months, depending on whether it is suitable for the country's conditions and whether it is in line with customs. Our country has been settling accounts according to the three festivals of the lunar calendar for thousands of years. It should be changed gradually. It seems that during the period of political tutelage, we should temporarily set the end of January of the following year as the closing date for the previous year. This year, we should especially extend it by 15 days. During these four or five years, we should try our best to implement it and gradually change the example of settling accounts by festivals to settling accounts annually, and then to settling accounts monthly. Perhaps the time is sufficient, and reform is not difficult. At that time, we will reconsider the situation and discuss it at length. If changing to settling accounts at the end of the year is not difficult, then we will follow the end of the year uniformly. Otherwise, we will set a separate fiscal year for commercial affairs to ensure that politics and commerce do not interfere with each other and instead help each other appropriately. Although the association is not involved in politics, it should be discussed from a practical point of view. In addition to sending separate letters to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Money Industry Association, I respectfully propose the following. I respectfully request your approval for implementation and instruct compliance for the benefit of the public. Respectfully submitted to Pan, Director of the Shanghai Social Bureau.

Export Freight for European Lake Silk Soars 115

▲ Unprecedented Export Silk Costs

The slump in the Chinese silk industry this year is unprecedented. The number of silk mills in Shanghai that have suspended operations has reached 106. The export volume of Chinese silk has also been affected. Recently, the number of silk shipments exported by British and French postal ships has sharply decreased. It is reported that there are only about 2,000 silk pieces stored in Shanghai. This situation is rare in recent years. However, British and French postal shipping companies have suddenly increased the export freight for Lake silk during this period of slump in the silk industry. The freight per piece has increased by a huge amount of several taels of silver per 112 pounds. The freight for transporting silk has always fluctuated by only two or three cents of silver per piece and has never increased so dramatically as it does now. It truly breaks the historical record for export silk freight. The freight for transporting silk from Shanghai to Europe was 14 taels, 9 mace, and 5 fen per piece in October of the year before last. It had risen to 17 taels by October of last year. Now, it has suddenly increased to 26 taels and 6 mace. The freight for yellow silk was only 11 taels and 6 mace on this day the year before last. Last year, it increased to 13 taels and 1 mace. This year, it has exceeded 20 taels, which is a huge price never seen before. The new prices are listed below, which are also closely related to the shipping industry.

Wheat Inspection Methods Have Been Resolved 116

▲ Effective from the 21st

▲ Inspection Will Be Implemented Universally

Regarding the inspection of wheat, the Shanghai Chinese Grain Association had previously submitted its opinions on various methods for organizing and inspecting wheat to the Shanghai Agricultural Products Inspection Office of the Ministry of Agriculture and Mines, requesting their adoption. They also sent representatives Ye Huijun and Cai Yukun to the office to discuss the methods. The authorities of the office received them and, after detailed explanations, reached a satisfactory agreement on the registration of existing goods and the inspection of new goods. At the request of the representatives, the date of inspection was postponed, and it was decided that all wheat arriving in Shanghai before October 20th of this year should be sent to the office for registration before October 20th. From October 21st, it is necessary to report to the office for inspection in accordance with the provisional measures for inspecting wheat. Both old goods and goods in transit will be handled as new goods.

The Cotton Exhibition Sends Letters Soliciting Exhibits 117

The Shanghai Exhibition Collection Office of the Cotton Textile Exhibition of the National Goods Exhibition Hall of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce sent a letter to the Shanghai National Goods Factory Federation and other five groups yesterday, stating: "Dear Sirs, our museum believes that cotton products are essential for the public's daily use. In order to promote frugality and thrift, we are hosting a cotton product exhibition to encourage and inspire learning. We have drafted the charter and rules for collecting exhibits and have submitted them to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for approval and have also sent letters appointing preparatory committee members and collection directors. To facilitate the collection of exhibits, we have specifically borrowed the Shanghai National Goods Factory Federation at 713 Jiu'an Lane, Wuma Road as the Shanghai Exhibition Collection Office. The exhibition will open on November 1st of this year and will last for one month, divided into two parts: display and sale. There are two types of sales: consignment and stall sales. Only a handling fee will be charged (the fee will be charged according to the size of the business and will be decided by the participating manufacturers at the representatives' conference). Other expenses such as electricity will be provided by the museum. Exhibits must be shipped before October 20th, and saleable goods must be shipped to Beijing before October 25th. The deadline is approaching, so we are writing to your association to send letters to the factories of each member, asking them to actively participate to support the grand event. We eagerly await your response."

Cessation of Transit Tax on Hunan Rice 118

▲ Ministry of Finance Has Ordered the Jianghan Customs to Exempt It

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Grain and Oil Cake Association yesterday stating: "We previously received a letter from Taiwan stating that the Jianghan Customs' collection of transit tax on Hunan rice arriving in Hankou hinders the people's food supply and requested that we forward a request to order the Hankou Customs to cancel the exemption. Our association immediately forwarded the request to the Ministry of Finance for review and handling. We have now received a true telegram from the Ministry of Finance stating that they have received the telegram and have ordered the Jianghan Customs to immediately exempt the transit tax on Hunan rice. Li Kebin Privately Detained His Wife 121

▲ She Was Rescued in a Near-Death State

▲ The Accumulation of Feces and Foul Odor

Is Li Tan's Mentally Ill?

Li Kebin, a native of Guangxi, resides at No. 826 Pingliang Road, Yangshupu. Between the 9th and 13th of this month, he inexplicably and secretly detained his wife, Li Tan, in the attic of the house, locking the door and depriving her of food and drink, intending to starve her to death. The second landlord, Zhang Jiaping, a native of Ningbo, advised Li in vain. He also did not understand the truth of what they did due to the language barrier. Fearing that she would starve to death inside without reporting it to the police, he could not shirk his responsibility as the landlord. However, Li insisted that it was okay, saying that his wife would definitely not die. Therefore, Zhang would hit her window with a wooden pole from the sun deck every morning and evening. When she heard the sound, she approached the window and asked Zhang to buy bread and boiled water to satisfy her hunger. At 5:00 PM the day before yesterday, a neighbor, Chinese Constable No. 2160 from Sandaotou, Yangshupu Police Station, met Zhang and learned of the matter. He reported it to the police station. The police chief sent Western Detective Mek accompanied to the address, opened the attic, and saw her lying in bed, in a near-death state and about to die. The room was full of feces and foul odor, which was unbearable. They immediately found a way to hire a car to take her to the hospital for treatment and detained Li Kebin in the police station. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Third Criminal Court of the Special District Court. According to the police station's lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, he stated the case and said that the police station accused the defendant of attempted murder under Article 282, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law. The victim, Li Tan, is a native of Guangxi and there is no one to translate today. Please postpone the case. Then, the Chinese Constable from Sandaotou and the Western Detective successively reported the situation at the time. Zhang Jiaping, the second landlord, also provided a testimony. Li Tan was able to say that she was 40 years old and made gestures with her hands. The rest of her words were unclear. When questioned, the defendant Li Kebin, speaking Cantonese, confessed that she had recently suffered a major episode of mental illness and insulted and beat people she met. Therefore, the nanny who had already returned to her hometown locked her in the room. He ordered people to give her food and drink through the side windows and did not intend to starve her to death. His concubine, Li Zhou, also stated that Tan had indeed suffered from her old illness, so the nanny locked her in the room and she sent her food and drink every day. Judge Ge Zhitan reviewed the confession and ordered the defendant to be remanded in custody and the hearing postponed for seven days. Li Tan should be sent to the hospital by the police station for examination.

Yesterday's Continued Hearing of Zhang Nai's Bigamy Case 122

▲ Yang Xuejiu Was Watched by the Crowd

▲ Zhang Nai's Whereabouts Are Also Unknown

▲ The Court Ordered Another Hearing Next Wednesday

The bigamy case of You Yaohao against Zhang Nai, etc., was continued yesterday at the Special District Court. The presiding judge was Cheng Shangfeng. After 1:00 PM, Criminal Court No. 2 was already full, with more men than women. Yang Xuejiu is the second defendant in the case and is also the main figure in the case. After several hearings, she has been called for many times. Apart from attending the second instance, she has not been present. Yesterday, she had to attend because the attorney, Jiang Yiping, had repeatedly asked her to do so. Yang's appearance is not bad, with willow eyebrows, almond eyes, snow-white skin, and a bridge on her nose, probably due to myopia. Her shiny hair was styled in a childish manner. She wore a coat and silk stockings with a cheongsam. After entering the court, attorney Jiang asked her to sit in the translator's seat. Later, because the seats were quite crowded, she got up and went to the reporter's seat and whispered to her younger sister. Her voice was very low, and no one could hear it. At this time, many of the onlookers knew that she was Yang Xuejiu, who had not attended several court sessions. Thus, she attracted much attention. After 2:00 PM, Judge Cheng took the stand, and You Yaohao walked to the plaintiff's column. Her mother sat next to her. The court also summoned Yang Xuejiu and Gong Yu to come forward. Yang Xuejiu's mother hired a lawyer to represent her, saying that Yang's mother had recently developed a tumor and could not attend the court. Judge Cheng also asked Yang Xuejiu where Zhang Nai was and asked if she had seen a quick letter that You Yaohao wrote to her mother on December 2nd of last year. After Yang read the letter, she said that she had not received it. On December 1st, she went to Beijing for business and returned after a week. Zhang Nai's whereabouts are also unknown. He also asked if she and Zhang Nai had a marriage certificate. She replied that because they were married in a church, they did not have a certificate. Judge Cheng then asked You Yaohao why the items in Gong Yu's possession had not been retrieved because there was no place to put them. The court pondered for a long time and then asked why the letter you posted at the Xujiahui branch on December 2nd of last year was stated to be sent on the 4th. You replied that he might have misremembered the date. At this point, the court ordered the case to be rescheduled for next Wednesday, ordering Zhang Nai to be arrested and summoning Pastor Yu to attend the court. Yang Xuejiu must pay additional bail. Yang looked displeased upon hearing the order. Attorney Jiang requested that the bail be waived, saying that his representative could be responsible for ensuring that Yang would be present at the next hearing. Judge Cheng then ordered that Yang pay a "ready to appear" bond.

A Brief Biography of the Tragically Deceased Industrialist Xu Wenhuan 124

The tragic death of Mr. Xu Wenhuan was reported yesterday. It is now known that Mr. Xu was the grandson of Mr. Xu Xuecun of Wuxi. During the Tongzhi and Guangxu eras of the Qing Dynasty, Mr. Xuecun translated books on chemistry and physics with Westerners, enlightening future generations and gaining renown at the time. His sons, Zhonghu and Zhusan, both carried on his work. The Xu family, father and sons, along with Mr. Hua Ruoting of the same county, were listed in the National History Museum's biographies, and the villagers respected them as the Four Sages of Wuxi. Wenhuan was born to Zhusan and received a strict education from his family, excelling in learning, especially in technology. For the past twenty years, he established the Gaoyi Company on Gaochang Temple Longhua Road, manufacturing electrical appliances and artificial ice, among other things. Merchants competed to buy them. He was diligent and thrifty, liked to supervise construction, and personally took charge of the work. On the thirteenth, while inspecting a motor, he accidentally severed his left arm and died before he could be saved. It is truly lamentable. It is recalled that Mr. Xu Zhonghu served as the superintendent of the Hanyang Arsenal during the late Qing Dynasty, manufacturing cotton gunpowder, and died in an explosion. Both a son and a grandson of Mr. Xuecun died because of learning, which can be said to be a great misfortune for Chinese entrepreneurs.
