Detailed Record of the Shareholders' Meeting of Dasheng Factories One, Two, and Three 127

▲ Factory One: The shareholders' meeting of Dasheng Factory One was held on the eleventh of this month at the Bank Association. Shareholders representing a total of 8,686 shares attended, and Mr. Li Qiqing was elected chairman. The formalities were performed as usual. Then, Chairman Zhang Xiaoshi reported on the progress of the factory. Supervisors Yun Jishen and Chen Zixiang reported on the accounts. Committee member Zhou Meiquan reported on the beginning and end of the committee's task. Next, several proposals were made. Shareholder Yang raised three questions: (1) Why has the shareholders' meeting been held only now after four years? (2) The formation of the maintenance association and its contract should be announced. (3) Although the business has made a profit, why is it not as good as other factories? The manager should be responsible for answering this question. The chairman said that the three matters that Shareholder Yang requested to be answered were all past events. Of course, there are facts. It is best to ask shareholders to save this precious time and pay more attention to future matters to seek benefits for the company. Wu Jiyun said, "I am responsible for the Shanghai office. I remember the past events in more detail. Today, I cannot help but answer a few words briefly to dispel the shareholders' doubts." (1) The board of directors has repeatedly proposed the shareholders' meeting, but there were unavoidable considerations. It was still for the sake of maintaining the company. Then, it was delayed due to handling registration procedures. As for the maintenance association contract and the new and old accounts of the syndicate, Director Zhang of the former Finance Department sent a supervisor to reside in the factory. Director Wang of the Construction Department also sent a section chief to the company for an investigation. Both departments have copies, and there are no secrets. As for the thin profits, Manager Li has already reported on it, but he is now recuperating at Mogan Mountain. I cannot give a detailed answer on the matters in the factory. Official shareholder representative Jin Baoguang said, "This time, the provincial government has appointed me and Cheng Baitang, Guan Ji'an, Shen Yanmou, and Chen Guangfu to be candidates for directors and supervisors on behalf of the official shares of the company. I am able to participate in today's shareholders' meeting and meet with all the shareholders. All the official documents of the provincial government have just been announced by the chairman. Since Dasheng was founded in the eleventh year of the Republic of China, there have been many problems that cannot be solved immediately. We can only hope that the reorganized board of directors, directors and supervisors, can all be the right people and work together to improve the company. The purpose of the provincial government's appointment of us and our future tasks for the company are all in this. There are many proposals listed on today's agenda, and some of them can be discussed by the new board of directors in the future in order to solve them. Those that must be discussed by the shareholders' meeting at present should be put forward for discussion immediately. After the discussion is completed, the weight should be measured extremely heavily, and the directors and supervisors should be elected first to facilitate the process." Then, Zhou Meiquan, Wu Yunshang, and other gentlemen seconded the motion and expressed their opinions. As a result, the motion was passed to add shares from previous profits, and the case of Zhuang Xi's case was transferred to the eight-factory share capital and issued long-term deposit slips. Then, nine directors and three supervisors were re-elected. Jin Baoguang, Cheng Baitang, Zhang Xiaoruo, Wu Jichen, Gao Hefu, Li Qiqing, Xu Taoan, Zhao Shuyong, and Zhou Meiquan were elected as directors. Chen Guangfu, Fang Juchuan, and Yun Jishen were elected as supervisors.

▲ Factory Two: The shareholders' meeting of Factory Two was held at the Bank Association on the afternoon of the twelfth, attended by shareholders representing a total of 4,450 shares. Mr. Hu Kezhi was elected chairman, and the formalities were performed as usual. First, Chairman Zhang Xiaoruo reported on the company's situation and the company's revised mortgage contract, which had been agreed to by the creditors, and a discretionary payment was made to reorganize the machinery. Then, supervisors Li Bake and Zhang Dongfu reported on the accounts. Committee representative Zhou Meiquan reported on the beginning and end of the committee's assistance to the factory affairs. Later, Shareholder Wu distributed printed materials, questioning the borrowing and mortgaging of Factory Two by Factory One. Therefore, shareholders Yang Guanchang, Gu Shaoyi, etc. requested the chairman to explain the truth of the matter. Wu Jichen detailed the process of the matter and the reason why Dasheng factories have always been consistent in their dealings with the outside world, and that they should help each other in times of difficulty. Zhou Meiquan, Shen Yanmou, Shen Zhihan, and others further explained, and all the shareholders suddenly realized. Then, directors and supervisors were elected. A total of seven directors were elected: Shen Yanmou, Wang Dankui, Xu Jingren, Zhang Xiaoruo, Zhang Dongfu, Xu Jiyu, and Zhou Zishan were elected. Two supervisors, Li Bake and Shen Kunsan, were elected.

▲ Factory Three: The shareholders' meeting of Factory Three was held at the same place on the thirteenth. Shareholders representing a total of 10,529 shares attended, and Mr. Hu Kezhi was elected chairman. The formalities were performed as usual. Board of directors representative Zhang Xiaoruo reported on the progress of the factory. Committee representative Zhou Meiquan reported on the beginning and end of the committee's task. Next, regarding the proposed matters, Shareholder Li inquired about the current profit situation. Director Wu Jichen explained on the spot that although the current profit is 200,000 taels, it is difficult to distribute it to shareholders because there is a contract with the syndicate to repay the debt first. In the future, the new board of directors can discuss with the syndicate to extract a portion of the profit and distribute dividends. After a long discussion by shareholders such as Zhang Chuba, Zhou Meiquan, and Zhao Hansheng, the consensus was that the bank must be required to retain a portion of the surplus, or add shares to pay off a small amount of debt, so that dividends can be issued as soon as possible. It was resolved: (1) To instruct the new board of directors to do its best to consult with the creditors and revise the mortgage contract, so that a portion of the surplus will be used to repay the debt, and a portion will be used to distribute dividends. (2) To add 220,000 taels of shares to make up the share capital to 2.5 million taels. Then, directors and supervisors were elected. Wu Tingfan, Zhang Xiaoruo, Guan Ji'an, Shen Yanmou, Wu Jichen, Yang Dunfu, and Zhou Weibin were elected as directors. Chen Zixun and Li Yunhou were elected as supervisors.

Cai Linzhen Sues for Divorce 128

Cai Gensheng, a local resident, lives at No. 161, Zhilu, South Railway Station, and makes a living by farming. He has only one daughter, named Linzhen, who is currently nineteen years old. On December 12th of last year, she was married to Zhu Qiuyan, the son of Zhu Wu, residing at No. 28, Tianzhutang Street, Maluqiao, through a matchmaker. Not long after she entered the family, the couple developed disagreements due to money issues, leading to frequent conflicts. The mother-in-law and daughter-in-law also fell out of favor because of this. Now, Cai Linzhen has hired lawyer Liu Xiang to file a divorce lawsuit in the local court. The reason is that she was abused and driven out by the defendant Zhu Qiuyan and his mother, Zhu Wu, and that the plaintiff's dowry was moved and hidden elsewhere. She requests permission to divorce and return all the dowry and compensation of 700 yuan. Because the plaintiff is only nineteen years old, her father, Cai Gensheng, is also listed as her legal representative. Yesterday morning, Judge Zhang Jinjian specially opened the Ninth Tribunal to hear the case. The defendant Zhu Qiuyan was absent, and only Zhu Wu appeared in court. After the judge took the seat, he first took the plaintiff Cai Linzhen's statement of the events. (Question) What are you requesting? (

Page 16

Answer) Because I have been repeatedly oppressed by the defendants, I request permission to divorce and request the return of the dowry worth 1,277 yuan. (Question) How many requests do you have? (Answer) There are four points in total. (1) Request for divorce. (2) Return of the dowry. (3) Compensation, that is, alimony of 700 yuan. (4) The costs of this case should be borne by the defendant. (Question) Why are you suing Zhu Wu? (Answer) Because all the property is managed by Zhu Wu, and she said that since I entered the family last December until January this year, the defendant Zhu Qiuyan asked me for gold jewelry and ordered me to borrow 3,000 yuan from my mother's relatives. I went home to discuss with my parents, who thought the amount was too large and could not be borrowed at once. Before long, Qiuyan ordered me to return to my mother's house and borrowed 200 yuan. In June, Qiuyan wanted to ask me to borrow money from my mother's house but could not, so he beat me and moved the dowry to Zhang Tinggui's house. After I returned to my mother's house, he did not come to pick me up. (Question) What is the relationship between this Zhang Tinggui? (Answer) It is said that he is an adoptive grandfather. I don't know how. My husband and mother-in-law both listen to him. I don't know why. Next, the defendant Zhu Wu stated that she is 46 years old, from Shanghai, and that Zhu Qiuyan is my son. He is currently in Hangzhou collecting debts, so he is not here. The young couple usually get along very well and have never fought, but there have been quarrels. (Question) Was there any borrowing? (Answer) No. After my daughter-in-law returned to Ning in June this year, she left and never returned. (Question) Is the plaintiff's dowry still there? (Answer) It is still there. All the items sent to other places are my daughter's dowry and my belongings, not my daughter-in-law's dowry. (Question) Your daughter-in-law is requesting a divorce. What is your opinion? (Answer) I don't want to. I am a poor person. It is not easy to marry a daughter-in-law. I taught my son that he must first greet his daughter-in-law and not be too suspicious. I treat my daughter-in-law the same as I treat my daughter, etc. Then, Cai Gensheng stated that he is 41 years old. (Question) Why don't you persuade your daughter not to divorce? (Answer) I have persuaded my daughter, but it is really because she has been repeatedly abused. My daughter's divorce from her son-in-law is also embarrassing for me. The judge ordered Zhu Qiuyan to be summoned to court for trial and adjourned the court.

Regulations for the Management of Public Entertainment Venues 129

▲ Announced Yesterday by the Municipal Government

The municipal government believes that the management of public entertainment venues must be responsible for protecting public safety and tranquility, and suppressing practices that harm social morality and progress. Therefore, it has specially formulated the Shanghai Municipal Public Entertainment Venue Management Regulations, which were announced yesterday.

▲ Shanghai Municipal Public Entertainment Venue Management Regulations. Article 1: All game venues, local opera venues, storytelling venues, theaters, cinemas, dance halls, and other public entertainment venues established within the city of Shanghai shall comply with these regulations. Article 2: To establish a public entertainment venue, an application must be made to the Public Security Bureau for a business license before business can be opened. Article 3: Business licenses cannot be transferred. The performances and business location are limited to what has been approved in the application. This license must be returned immediately on the day of closure. If the location is moved, a separate application must be submitted for the issuance of a business license. Article 4: If a public entertainment venue fails to start business within one month after obtaining a business license, or suspends business halfway for more than two weeks, the license may be revoked, except in special circumstances with the approval of the Public Security Bureau. Article 5: After obtaining a business license, public entertainment venues shall, based on the certificate, pay the monthly donation for the business license to the Finance Bureau before the 15th of each month, in accordance with the regulations. Those who are overdue until after the 1st of the following month will be punished in accordance with the regulations. Article 6: The business license shall be hung in a place easily accessible to the public for inspection. Article 7: All public entertainment venues shall pay attention to the following hygiene matters: (1) The air in the venue must be circulated. Ventilation equipment shall be installed in necessary places. In each theater, doors and windows must be opened once every hour. The opening time must be at least five minutes. (2) The venue shall be kept strictly clean, and more spittoons and signs stating "No Spitting on the Ground" shall be provided. (3) Those with attached kitchens must pay special attention to cleanliness and install gauze cabinets, gauze windows, and gauze doors to prevent mosquitoes and flies. (4) All public entertainment venues, except cinemas, shall have sufficient light. (5) Each venue shall have sufficient toilets and shall be cleaned and swept frequently, and disinfectant and deodorant shall be sprayed to maintain cleanliness. (6) Unclean and unboiled water shall not be provided to tourists. All drinking utensils shall be immersed in boiling water or disinfected after each use before being reused. (7) Public towels shall be washed, boiled, and disinfected for five minutes after each use before being reused. Article 8: Business hours (except for dance halls, which are open until 1:00 AM in spring and winter, and until 2:30 AM in summer and autumn) shall not be later than 12:00 PM. Article 9: If there is any illegal behavior in the venue, the person in charge of the venue shall report it to the local district office of the Public Security Bureau for handling at any time. Article 10: The construction of public entertainment venue buildings shall comply with the provisions of the city's building regulations. Those that have been transformed from ordinary houses must be demolished and rebuilt if the Public Works Bureau deems them unqualified. All houses that are too old or cannot be transformed shall be banned. Article 11: All water and electricity equipment in public entertainment venues shall be handled in accordance with the city's various water and electricity regulations. Article 12: The scripts and plays for performances shall comply with the following provisions: (1) All rehearsals shall be submitted by the playwrights, along with the content of the play, four copies of the application form, and two copies each of the script (or explanation) and the list of actors, to the Education Bureau for review. After approval, a license shall be issued before the performance can be performed, and the Education Bureau shall notify the Public Security and Social Bureaus for investigation and reference. (2) All performance licenses that have passed the review shall be hung in the performance venue. (3) Performances with any of the following circumstances shall not be performed: (a) Those that violate party principles and insult the national system. (b) Those that endanger morality and public safety. (c) Those that promote superstition, heresy, and feudal ideology. (4) If there are any changes in the name or content of the performances that have been approved for rehearsal, they shall be reported in advance for future reference. (5) If it is found that the performances that have been approved for rehearsal are far from or inconsistent with what is stated in the original application form, they shall be stopped immediately. (6) The Education Bureau may send personnel to inspect and guide and correct public entertainment venues during performances at any time. Article 13: If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, they may be amended at any time. Article 14: These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation by the Municipal Government.

New Lung Hospital to Build Bone Tuberculosis Hospital 130

The Lung Disease Sanatorium at No. 2 and No. 4, Great West Road, Shanghai, in view of the recent global methods of treating lung diseases, has moved away from the inherent internal medicine scope, and uses surgical methods of treatment to directly compress lung cavities and achieve complete cure. The hospital, in view of the increasing number of people using surgery to treat lung diseases, and the large number of Chinese people suffering from surgical tuberculosis, has built a bone tuberculosis hospital, because the original second and third hospitals are insufficient to accommodate them. Dr. Engel, a German surgeon and orthopedic expert, and Dr. Huang Dinghu, are the chief directors. Construction has been underway for nearly a year. All

The construction and internal equipment were completed yesterday. There are lung surgery rooms and electrical lung treatment rooms. The interior of the new hospital is completely a very pleasing light yellow color. The ward equipment is also different in each room. The windows have been specially enlarged, and the light and air are extremely sufficient. Each room has a water temperature regulator. The flying springs, sunken fish, flowers and trees in the garden are quiet and beautiful. It can be called a good place for recuperation in Shanghai. The image on the left is the front of the new hospital. It is heard that the hospital's medical affairs are becoming more and more busy, and from today, German lung disease expert Dr. Feinerhi will be hired to visit the hospital for consultation.

Ship Collision, Helmsman Falls into Water 132

▲ Due to Rapid Tide and Swift Current, He Has Likely Drowned

▲ Yang Xueheng's Body Has Not Yet Been Recovered

Recently, the northeast wind has been strong, and the tide has been high. Yesterday was supposed to be a minor flood tide, but the tide was no different from a major flood tide. The water flow was very swift, and the water color was muddy red. At half past one yesterday afternoon, the Ningbo salted crab boat "Xi He Xing" was docked at the Pujiang Riverbank of Wusong East Wharf. The helmsman, Yang Xueheng, 32 years old, from Ningbo, bought an iron anchor ashore and hired a sampan to row to the side of the crab boat. While Yang was carrying the iron anchor onto the boat, he lost his footing due to the surge of the tide, and he and the anchor fell into the center of the river together. Although the sampan crew tried to rescue him, the tide was too swift and the current too rapid. In a short time, he disappeared completely, presumably having drowned. The boat crew reported the incident to Shunfa Tax Reporting Agency, and they are currently trying to recover the body.

Li Linfa (also known as Yu San), a local resident, was previously arrested by Chief Detective Mao Yiwen of the Hongkou Police Station and others for repeatedly committing major crimes. Recent News on the Joint Defense of Four Counties 136

The joint defense of Shanghai, Nanhui, Songjiang, and Fengxian counties has held two meetings to resolve all matters and has passed the joint defense regulations, which have been submitted to the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department for review. Proclamation on the Cessation of Collecting Defense Corps Donations 137

The Shanghai Municipal Defense Corps Reorganization Committee issued a proclamation yesterday, stating: "Regarding the matter of this proclamation, all teams under the former Shanghai Songhu Defense Corps have been taken over and reorganized by this committee as ordered. The voluntary donations previously contributed by local merchants and residents in the Hunan and Zhabei districts to the defense corps have also been ordered by this committee to cease collection. No fundraising is allowed under any pretext. However, we have heard that some unscrupulous individuals are daring to impersonate the defense corps and continue to collect donations as before. Merchants and residents, unaware of this, have fallen victim to their fraud and regard it as a regular contribution, which is deeply regrettable. It should be known that the regular expenses of all teams under this committee are approved by the Shanghai Municipal Government and disbursed monthly by the Municipal Finance Bureau to each district team. If expenses are economized, there is no need to worry about shortages and no need to solicit donations, which would cause disturbance and burden. Therefore, we solemnly declare that if anyone is found falsely claiming to be the Hunan or Hubei teams of the defense corps, or any team under them, and soliciting voluntary donations from local merchants and residents, they should be reported by name or detained. This committee will investigate and punish them severely according to the law, without leniency. For fear of insufficient information, this proclamation is hereby issued."

Chinese Vessels Gather in Xunbu Along the Yangtze River 138

▲ Decline in Trade Between Jiangxi and Shanghai

▲ Sluggish Passenger and Freight Traffic to Xunbu

Navigation on the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, in the Jiujiang area, has recently been subject to stricter precautions. Moreover, the import and export of goods in Jiangxi Province have declined sharply. The recent situation is described below:

▲ Jiangxi Rice Stopped Coming: In the past ten days, the export of rice from Jiangxi has been stopped. Therefore, the arrival of Jiangxi rice to Shanghai has been nonexistent in recent days. The reason for the suspension is due to local unrest, causing a temporary halt to shipments. Therefore, the Guang Gang (Guangdong Merchants) has turned to Wuhu, buying 180,000 bags of rice to be shipped to Guangdong, having chartered the Longshan ship, which is scheduled to depart today. All Jiangxi rice is temporarily not loaded.

▲ Departure Goods Greatly Reduced: After the Mid-Autumn Festival, the Jiangxi Gang (Jiangxi Merchants) sent telegrams to Shanghai, ordering a temporary halt to the loading of large quantities of goods for export to Jiangxi. As a result, in recent days, the outbound trips of British and Japanese Yangtze River vessels have seen a sharp decline in cargo bound for Jiujiang. Yesterday, the outbound cargo carried by Jardine Matheson and Nisshin Kisen's Yangtze River vessels and unloaded in Jiujiang for overland transport amounted to only 176 pieces. It seems that the goods that have been prepared are too afraid to be loaded.

▲ Vessel Precautions: British and Japanese Yangtze River vessels, averaging five or six daily navigating the Yangtze River, face frequent dangers in the Xunhan section. Therefore, the naval escorts for each vessel have been increased by two additional soldiers, totaling more per ship. Approaching Jiujiang, the soldiers prepare their guns. In the Xunhan section, in addition to British and Japanese warships patrolling to protect vessel traffic, China's Yangtze River Fleet has been requested to dispatch three additional warships to assist.

▲ Merchant Vessels Gather in Xunbu: The Chinese merchant vessels suspending operations initially numbered ten, distributed across Hankou and Nanjing. Beginning last week, all have been dispatched to Jiujiang. Vessels such as "Gongping," "Taishun," "Jiangtian," "Jiahe," "Yongxing," "Fulong," "Dexing," etc., all arrived in Jiujiang from Pukou within the past week. Just after these vessels arrived in Xunbu, China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, Sanpei Steam Navigation Company, and others dispatched an additional eight Jianghai vessels, including "Jiangxin" and "Huayang," all sailing to Jiujiang. Consequently, there are now seventeen or eighteen merchant vessels suspending operations in Jiujiang, gathered at that port.

Those Who Arrange Passports for Peddlers to Go Abroad 139

▲ Municipal Public Security Bureau Conducting Strict Investigations

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has repeatedly received telegrams from Minister Jiang in Germany and Minister Gao in France, stating that there are many Chinese peddlers abroad, hawking on the streets and resembling beggars, which is detrimental to the national image. In addition to taking steps to compel them to return home, they requested that the provincial and municipal governments be consulted to strictly crack down on the issuance of passports to these peddlers and impose restrictions. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has consulted the Shanghai Municipal Government, instructing the passport-issuing agencies to comply. Since the strict crackdown, peddlers seeking to go abroad to do business have been scheming everywhere. Some have even traveled to the Guangdong Municipal Government to apply for passports. Some, such as so-and-so, who specialize in arranging passports for these peddlers, have devised a plan to smuggle them abroad, halving the cost of the boat fare per person and bribing the ship's crew to hide the peddlers in the engine room or dress them as sailors to impersonate crew members. These peddlers and merchants are willing to hide anywhere, as long as they can reach their destination. Although they are sometimes discovered by the shipping company and ordered ashore, they continue to try. Now, the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau has learned that these "dai ke" (agents), who only care about their own profits, are extremely despicable. It is sending personnel to secretly investigate and punish them according to the law.

▲ Ant-Matchmaker Mo Fusheng Caught

Mo Fusheng, a famous ant-matchmaker residing near Yu Botitian Bridge in Pudong, was arrested by the Fourth Branch of the Sanlintang County Public Security Bureau in January of this year for a case involving the enticement of women. Now, Mo, believing that several months had passed and the matter had subsided, secretly returned home. This was discovered by the Fourth Branch, which dispatched police to arrest him and send him to the Shanghai County Public Security Bureau. Yesterday, he was brought in for interrogation. Mo admitted to the escape but claimed that the handcuffs had been destroyed and discarded on the way, making it impossible to hand them over. The judge ordered him to be detained pending investigation and punishment by the court.

Weather Report 151

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the sky would be cloudy with fog, and the northeasterly wind in the East China Sea and the Taiwan Strait would be quite strong. Also, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 72.7 degrees, and the lowest was 62.8 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 83.3 degrees, and the lowest was 58.6 degrees.

Letter to the Editor 152

We recently saw in your newspaper's local news section a report stating that a shed belonging to the Futai Lumber Company on Caishi Road collapsed yesterday afternoon, severing electric wires and causing all the nearby lights to go out due to the power outage. Fortunately, no one was injured, etc. We were surprised and alarmed to read this. Upon investigation, the shed was actually hooked by a tram's iron pole and pulled down. Your newspaper's report that it "suddenly collapsed" completely obscures the fact that it was struck. Therefore, we hereby clarify this matter and request that it be published in the "Letters to the Editor" section for correction. This is our earnest request. Respectfully submitted to the Chief Editor of Shen Bao. Sincerely, Futai Lumber Company. October 14th.

Special Publication

Thank You to Supporters of the National Products Movement (Continuation 4) by Pan Gongzhan 153

From the above points, it is clear that the crux of the national products movement lies in the underdevelopment of production. To cure this underdevelopment, it is essential that all parties work together, openly and honestly, to find a solution. What are these areas that require the joint efforts of all parties? I will list them below, imitating the way a doctor prescribes medicine, in the form of a prescription for the revival of national products: (1) Labor-management cooperation: This is the first ingredient, used to dispel the vicious external evils. The illness has reached a point where strong medicine seems necessary. This requires both labor and management to cleanse their minds and openly cooperate to succeed. However, in the environment of the past two or three years, where problems have accumulated and become deeply ingrained, it is especially important for party branches and the government at all levels to take more responsibility, provide strong support, and carefully manage the situation. They should not be short-sighted and only consider the labor side, nor should they favor the capitalists in a way that leads to imbalances. Instead, they should guide both parties to understand the difficulties faced by national product factories and workers, ensuring that everyone operates within the bounds of the law and avoids deception. Only then can there be hope for recovery. It is especially important to severely punish those who obstruct cooperation, those "labor thieves" who exploit the labor movement for personal gain. (2) Reduce taxes and levies: This ingredient is used to nourish vital energy, and its importance is no less than the first. The responsibility for this lies entirely with the government, especially the financial authorities who control the power of taxation. There is an ancient saying, "draining the pond to catch all the fish." If the current heavy taxes and levies are not effectively reformed, we will reach a point where there are no fish left to catch. This method of killing the goose to get the golden eggs is not financial management. Without nurturing the source of tax revenue, only knowing how to increase taxes, the people's livelihood will naturally suffer more and more. We especially urge the government authorities to pay attention to the fact that tax rates should not favor foreign merchants at the expense of protecting Chinese merchants. They should reduce tax rates on national products while increasing taxes on foreign merchants. Even if a tariff protection policy cannot be implemented immediately, they should at least move in that direction. If our tax laws effectively protect foreign merchants, creating unequal treatment between Chinese and foreign businesses, it would be absurd. If the government does not substantially reduce taxes and levies, but merely issues empty promises to promote national products, the industrial and commercial sectors should rise up and urge them to take action. (3) Pool capital: This ingredient is also an essential tonic. The weak capital of domestic factories is insufficient to compete with domestic and foreign factories, let alone large foreign factories. As previously stated, industries like national product matches already feel the need to merge operations due to the heavy pressure from Swedish merchants. In fact, all national product businesses should quickly start by pooling capital to engage in larger-scale production. However, it is necessary for those in charge of companies to respect the law, ethics, and the rights of shareholders. Shareholders, on the other hand, should also not forget their own rights and responsibilities and should not allow managers to engage in fraud and self-enrichment. Only then can Chinese companies establish substantial credibility and use the name of a large company to attract large amounts of capital for centralized operation. If they continue to operate on a small scale individually, they will never be able to gain a foothold. (4) Scientific management: This seems like a foreign new medicine, something trendy doctors want to adopt. However, it is not adopted because it is trendy, but because it can improve the current management methods of domestic factories. Its purpose is to improve work efficiency and reduce unnecessary waste, which seems to be for the benefit of the capitalists. But at the same time, if management is effective and arrangements are appropriate, workers will not be overworked, and diligence will be rewarded accordingly. This is also for the benefit of the workers. Moreover, large-scale production, reduced costs, and lower prices benefit society as a whole, which is of great benefit to the general public. However, to use and administer this medicine, each factory must first have a foundation of labor-management cooperation and earnestly recruit talent. Only then can the medicine be administered correctly and its scientific effectiveness be demonstrated. Otherwise, if ignorant factory owners or managers use good names to excessively oppress and exploit workers' sweat and blood, calling it "scientific management," it will not only be useless but also harmful. This is similar to the story in a certain newspaper about a doctor in the countryside who used "aspirin" as a specific medicine for treating meningitis, deceiving villagers into swallowing it and delaying their treatment, resulting in death. This is another crime. (5) Rest and Recuperation: This is also a very important matter. For example, when facing a serious illness, rest and recuperation are needed. In addition to taking medicine, nursing care must also be appropriate. There must be an environment suitable for recuperation, allowing the patient to live in quiet isolation to recover. Otherwise, in the noisy city, mental and physical exhaustion will deepen the illness. The domestic industry and commerce are so depressed, partly due to the impact of war and banditry. The industrial and commercial sectors should know that without a unified government, there will be no peaceful situation, and without a peaceful society, it is impossible to develop industry. Therefore, for the present plan, we can only use our strength to promote unification, urge the government to implement reorganization and disarmament, strictly suppress bandits, eliminate the Communist Party, stabilize the local population, so that agricultural production can be revitalized, and transportation can be convenient. Then, after several years of rest and recuperation, the industry and commerce of national products will naturally gradually prosper. In short, the five ingredients mentioned above are all essential conditions for saving the fate of national products. If we sincerely hope for the development of national products and replace foreign goods, then the party branch, the government, and the industrial and commercial sectors should work together and share the responsibility, so that the national product production industry can gradually flourish, meet the needs of the Chinese people, and achieve self-sufficiency. Then, the general public's consumption will naturally be happy to adopt national products. In this National Products Movement Conference, in addition to encouraging the general public to purchase national products as much as possible, what we can offer in return to the enthusiastic supporters is only this sincere word: "Let us all work together to solve the difficulties facing the future of national products." September 25, 1930, in Shanghai. (End)

A Word of Wisdom 154

— Long

▲ The tongue survives through softness, the teeth are broken through opposition. Therefore, in our words and deeds, we should not be too sharp.

▲ If the art of returning to youth succeeds, the method of abstaining from grains will be essential. Otherwise, with limited resources and a growing population, the struggle among humans will inevitably intensify.

▲ Marriages arranged by matchmakers in the past were like playing hide-and-seek. Present-day free love has a speculative nature.

▲ The human heart is treacherous, and it is impossible to guard against everything. Only those who are indifferent to fame and gain can avoid all troubles.

▲ The day of marriage is the day love succeeds and also the day love breaks down.

▲ Half of the suicides in the world are indeed caused by harsh environments, and the other half are due to weak abilities.

▲ In the beginning of mutual admiration between men and women, there is an unspeakable joy in their hearts. Once married, they find it is nothing more than that.

▲ Children are the crystallization of the two sexes and the seeds of trouble. Because they not only add to your burden but also have the power to divide the love of the person in your heart.

▲ Cars are originally for busy people to travel, but the riders invariably want them to be fast and reach their destination in an instant. Even more people use them for joyrides as a fashion. No wonder news of car accidents often appears before our eyes.

▲ Occasionally, one or two foreign sailors are found on the road wearing Chinese melon-shaped hats. When Chinese people see them, they are all surprised. Looking back at the Chinese who wear Western suits and leather shoes, and felt hats and sticks, with a lively expression, I am afraid that the blue-eyed people are also secretly laughing.

Watching Autumn Dance Late at Night in Dahua 155

— Langgan

This year, the Liaoxi area suffered an extraordinarily severe flood. Zhang Hanqing, the chief administrator of the Northeast, was deeply concerned about it and repeatedly tried to find ways to provide relief. In Shanghai, the lead was taken by prominent figures such as Mr. Du Yuesheng, who initiated a charity performance by celebrities, which achieved remarkably impressive results. Following this was the unprecedented costume carnival organized by Dr. Zheng Yuxiu, which was held at the Dahua Hotel on Gordon Road two days after Double Ten Day. The meeting was originally scheduled to begin at nine o'clock, but by eight o'clock the venue was already packed. Those who arrived later continued to come in an endless stream. Dr. Zheng, having just recovered from enteritis, could not bear the fatigue, so her sister, Ms. Zheng Huichen, and others temporarily took over the arrangements. Mr. Yu Ziying, Yang Zhaoyun, Xu Yunxuan, and others coordinated everything, working very busily. Their enthusiasm was truly admirable.

▲ Golden Splendor: Before the opening ceremony, the municipal government's public security bureau military band played music, followed by a dance performance by the Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School. The five dancers were all dressed in gold-threaded garments, illuminated by electric lights, creating a dazzling and dreamlike effect. It was no wonder that applause arose from all around the venue.

▲ Bizarre and Colorful: Following this was a bizarre and colorful costume dance. Mr. Zhang Xiaolin and Mr. Wang Xiaolai were the most enthusiastic. Mr. Zhang wore a Western suit, a mask over his eyes, and a white beard attached to his mouth, looking exactly like a foreign deity of the land. Mr. Wang covered his eyes with black floral paper, revealing a slight smile on his face, and his steps were orderly, like those of a seasoned craftsman. Mrs. Feng Dengna wore a costume from the opera "Chun Xiang's Mischievous Schooling," looking remarkably like the character. Ms. Zheng Huichen dressed as Huang Tianba. It was said that her costume was prepared by Dr. Zheng, who originally intended to play the role herself but later had Ms. Huichen take over. As for the rest, the costumes were of all colors and varieties, too numerous to describe in detail.

▲ Melodious National Music: Next was the national music performed by the Datong Music Society. Previously, I had the opportunity to hear their elegant music at a garden party held by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and I described it with the words "bright moon and clear sky, gentle breeze." It was truly the sound of a peaceful and prosperous age. It was said that the establishment of the society received considerable support from Wang Xiaolai. That evening, Wang personally conducted, which shows his sincere appreciation.

▲ Grape Fairy: The Grape Fairy of the Star Film Company was one of the highlights of the event. This opera was originally a children's game, but now it was performed by adults. It seemed that the fairy had been upgraded to a great fairy. Hu Die played the fairy, her demeanor graceful and her voice particularly clear and bright. In the future, when it is made into a sound film, there will be much to rely on. Other female actors had delicate expressions, and the male actors added humor, both of which were beyond the capabilities of child actors. Zheng Qiu, Jian Yun, Hong Shen, Bu Gao, and others were on site to take care of things, acting as if they were directors.

▲ Famous Actors Singing and Dancing: Finally, famous actor Cheng Yanqiu performed the sword dance from "The Legend of Hong Fu." Cheng had already donated 2,000 yuan to the Liaoxi flood disaster at the request of the Beiping Relief Association. This time, he generously agreed to participate, completely voluntarily, which was admirable. During the sword dance, applause thundered. Many Westerners also valued it as worth watching, all marveling at it. At the end, due to audience demand, Cheng put in extra effort as it was a charity event, singing his masterpiece "Willow Welcoming Spring Nan Bangzi" to entertain the audience, almost every word was worth applause. That day happened to be Sunday, and the Grand Theatre had a daytime performance. Cheng performed both day and night. Although he was extremely tired, he was still so enthusiastic about the event. It was truly commendable.

A Record of Floating on Yuan Lake Under the Moonlight 156

— Deng Chunshu

My home is on the Baiyun Stream in Biling. Su Dongpo's old Purple Vine House and Yun Nantian's Ouxiang Old Hall are across the stream from each other. Singing and painting, all glory and shame are discarded. Having experienced the tragedy of Yuan Xiang this summer, I indulged even more in the pleasure of traveling the mountains. Yesterday, I traveled with Yu Lu on Qin Chuan, and hung Crane Yi from Su Men. As soon as I returned, the Ming Society comrades invited me to swim in Yuan Lake on the day before the Mid-Autumn Festival, to drink wine at the Yanyu Tower, and to hold a moonlit floating ceremony. So I transferred to Shanghai to go there. The poets of Jiangsu and Zhejiang who came to the meeting, young and old, were another twenty-two people. Such as Qingpu Xu Gongxiu, Wuxing Yao Diyuan, Hai Ning Chen Yitao, and Zhou Bianxi Daling from Hangzhou, Gu Xieguang’s chief secretary from Yue, Dai Boxin's father and son from, Zhu Dake took his eleven-year-old Xiao Ke. First came from Shanghai to take care of everything. The club title is Yuanhu Rafting Song, and Moonlit Night. So he opened the old brewing bamboo leaves, ate the famous dishes of Huili. One ship leisurely, good works one after another. Poetry chanted a hundred chapters. Lingge rose up. In the seat were only Wujiang Qinmu and I as painters. They were assigned to paint Zhu An’s Tansui and Yuanhu Fanyue. Title name Ben Juan first on the spot. Divided by seniority. Xiao Ke can also sing. Compensation and response are eloquent. They are all regarded as prodigies. At three o'clock, the boat reached Zhu An. An Zhuan originated from the Ming Dynasty. The courtyard has two trees of Taiwan Gui. Qiu Zhi is curved and has six or seven layers like a cover. More than sixteen feet high. Xin is a thing of three hundred years. Dake showed Jin Yong Lao Zhu Gu Wei. Titles long scrolls by famous people. It is also valuable. At three o'clock, I returned to the boat. I boarded Yanyu Tower together. It is in the water. It is like Xiaoyingzhou in West Lake. But the corridor and pavilion are uneven. The trees and rocks are towering. Looking at the lake and sky. Lingtang crab house. All into the painting. Then the setting sun on the water. The magical performance is over. Sumeru rises in the east. The smoke scene changed. The secluded reward is over time. Put in the middle stream. Eat plenty of Huling. Each chants good sentences. For example, Yao Zhang has 30 seven-character quatrains with upper and lower levels. Zhian's Fu Shui Tiao Ge Tou is also Yache. I only composed eight chapters. Then Zhuang Jingting and other six people returned to Shanghai. Yao Xuchen Wu. Go to Haining to watch the night tide. I and Ji Fan Xieguang Bianxi went to Hangzhou. Re-float on the moon lake. I had a picture of Autumn Rafting in Taihu Lake in October two years ago. There is a picture of spring rafting in Wuhu Lake in February. There are already pictures of Lantingshu on it. All are well-known in Jiang Zhe Yilin. Or eighteen people. Or more than twenty people. There are registration marks. Deng Zhuben talks about it. And combine it with today's tour. The picture will be completed. Early in the morning, I traveled to Tai Dai Lu Yue. Tiantai Yandang returned. I have completed one hundred and sixty paintings and poems of winning travels. I once composed a seven-character poem in the rhyme of Wushan. Now in the car. He also composed a poem about the Five Lakes. I floated over Poyang Lake and rafted in Taihu Lake. I had finished swimming in Shang Lake and Yuan Lake again. I came to Qinshui to sing in the Guiyuan Garden. I sang and wrote in Lanting for a mirror lake. Sitting with books to pass the years. Travel to see traces in Jianghu. Tomorrow I will go to West Lake again. Enjoy the Mid-Autumn Festival and drunk Moon Lake together. Poem completed. Xie Guang said. It is truly an innovation in seven-character poems. It can also be said to be a new chant of lakes and mountains. The car arrived in Hangzhou. Write this note to feed the readers. (No compensation)

Sitting in the Huaguang Tongle Meeting 157

— Zhou Shixun

When the past of life comes to the time of "recollection" and "discrimination", all the joy seems to be full of sorrow. I feel this every time. And I hope that I will have less happy life now. Lest the stone city of sorrow hinder my future.

The National Day seems to be worth my revelry. But sitting in the Huaguang Tongle Club in Dahua Hotel. Seeing the dance and hearing the music. As if they were hugging sharp swords and stabbing them into my ears. This is probably a special feeling. I think there will be no second discovery among the crowd sitting in the same field.

But I am not numb. I also applauded and praised Wang Qingxun's harmonica. Liang Saizhen's Cantonese opera. It's just from Ms. Liang's singing. I felt the loss of her youth again. And I worry about the general young girls.

Mr. Li Diyun is a strong general of the Lianqing Society. Thanks to his arrangement, this amusement is well-organized. He met me. He said to me. Have you been away from Shanghai for a long time? Yes. In fact, I have never left Shanghai, which is full of troubles. It's just that I can't feel interested in the lively gatherings. Alas, prosperous Shanghai. It's just a "river of troubles" in front of my eyes.

Lin Zecang is my old friend. His spirit of doing things is worth my admiration. But every time I see him being criticized by outsiders. It gave me a strange idea. People all over the world who love to do public affairs will inevitably have to pay for their own money to listen to gossip. After all, which career can make everyone feel satisfied? Probably first-class smart people can't find this answer either.

Alas, life, alas, happiness. Can't stand reminiscing. Can't stand discriminating. Try a little bit of the pleasure in front of you. Avoid a share of future sorrow. This is what I got from the clear songs and beautiful dances in the Dahua Tongle Meeting. I don't hope that people will express sympathy. I just hope that people will make the same distinction as me.

Notes on Italian Art Studies (1) 158

— Wang Yachen

▲ Fine Arts in Florence Before and After the Renaissance

In the early Renaissance in Italy in the fifteenth century, painting was centered in Florence. At that time, artists from all directions came one after another. Famous writers. At that time, they also used their personal skills in Florence. Just like the current painters. I have to go to Paris. So the Florentine style at that time. Blow all over Italy. With such a glorious history. Once in that place. For the artistic relics left behind in the past. It makes us have endless reference. Every street corner. There is no place without traces of art. A traveler. Stepped on the land of Florence. There is no place that makes you feel uncomfortable. Especially for people who study fine arts.

Although the birthplace of art is far away in Greece and Egypt. But the most brilliant art flower that blooms in the art world. You have to start with Florence. The building there, painting, sculpture, is still a concentrated place. People in Europe who practice art. I have to go to pay my respects. I came to Europe to study art. There are too many places I want to run. It wasn't until late April this year that I arrived in Florence.

The group of beast painters said. Modern artists. There is no need to take the relics of the ancients as a guise. Just pursue nature and your own heart. But art cannot be separated from tradition. There is temptation from predecessors. There is more enlightenment from many people. Suppose the art galleries of various countries. All burned with fire. I think the artists in Europe who claim to be creative now. Will be wandering. After I studied the art of Florence before and after the Renaissance. Can't help but say something. Special notes to tell the people of the country.

(1) Uffizi Museum. This museum was formerly the private residence of the Italian Duke Offizi. Since 1560. Changed to Art Museum. The Duke's name is still in use today. The museum is located in the city of Fobu. In front is the Vecchio Ancient Palace. Later, it faces the beautiful Fiume River. The museum displays more than 40 paintings and sculptures. His works were first collected by Medici. In recent decades, fine products from all over the world have been collected within. Now it has become one of the world's famous art museums. From the height of the Renaissance to the end of the sixteenth century. All Florentine art. The museum is especially rich. The works of famous artists in central and southern Italy are also gathered in the museum. There are also Holland. Spain. Famous French works from the sixteenth to nineteenth centuries. Divided into several rooms.

Enter the museum and go up the stairs on the right. There is a large room on the second floor. Hundreds of woodcut prints are on display. And there are many works by famous woodcut printmakers from modern countries. Woodcut printing is very popular in European countries now. Each art museum. There are decorations. Only the one displayed in the Offizi Museum. For the most complete.

Warmth in My Heart (293) 159

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 14: Emerald Bamboo Tears Stain the Woman's Broken Heart, the Fragrance of Red Lotus Fades and the Soul of a Girl Departs

Lianxiang was a good-natured person. She thought her destiny was to be a concubine. Even if the main wife was fierce, she would just lower her head and be a little obedient, and it would pass. She always looked at the master's face in everything. Now, the one we marry is the master, not the main wife. As long as the master is easy to talk to, he can take care of everything. Besides, before marrying Lianxiang, she saw him often returning late at night, without showing any fear of the people at home. Therefore, Lianxiang didn't take it to heart. Moreover, they didn't live in the same house. They were renting a small mansion outside. When she first entered the household, everyone said the situation was very good. Although they had deceived the female tiger, there were no flaws. However, after a few months, the people at home gradually found out. But they still didn't know where their small mansion was. They only knew that the master had taken a woman outside. How did the news leak out? It was said that it was spread by the servants. It turned out that Master Yin often went out in a carriage. The coachman was called Gensheng. Of course, he was Master Yin's confidant. No one else knew where Master Yin went every day, but the coachman Gensheng knew everything. Relying on the master having this secret agency, he also earned a lot of extra money. The master often told him not to talk nonsense at home. He casually told him, but he was a little uneasy. There was no way but to use money to shut his mouth. His wages were a given. He often overspent several months' wages. When he went to the accounting room to get his wages, the accountant refused to pay. He even argued with the accountant. The accountant had no choice but to ask the master for instructions. The master said, "Let him get a month's wages this time. He's not allowed to overspend again." In fact, the master was a little afraid of him. Later, he had to tell him, "Don't go to the accounting room to get your wages. Tell me when you need money." So he often said, "Gensheng, your cotton robe is not good to wear anymore. Go buy a new one." He also said, "Your hat and shoes are broken. Go buy a new hat and a new pair of shoes." Giving him ten or eight dollars was common. However, that Gensheng later hooked up with Aunt Jin, the main wife's hairstylist. Gensheng would naturally not reveal a word to others. But to Aunt Jin, he could no longer keep that secret. One day, Aunt Jin mentioned that the master was afraid of the main wife. Gensheng snorted in his nose and said, "Women are useless. How can they follow men all day long? No matter how fierce a woman is, the man will turn his back and trick her. They don't know that." Aunt Jin said, "Does the master also trick her?" Gensheng said, "Why not? He doesn't make a sound at home. When he goes outside, he laughs and talks. You see him being so proper at home. When he goes to the brothel, the girls and older sisters all want to welcome him. If you happen to go to the brothel, the master will also welcome you."

Financial and Monetary Market: Clear, Just, and Peaceful 160

▲ Swap Nearing Expiry

▲ General Attitude: Watching and Waiting

▲ Fluctuations Limited to Two Taels: Yesterday, the 14th, the gold market was in a state of hovering. There were fluctuations of about two taels before and after the market opening, but no particular gains or losses. This was mainly because the swap period was approaching, and the exchange rate was calculated at under 50 taels per day. Both buyers and sellers were adopting a neutral attitude. Foreign exchange seemed to be tight, with many transactions among banks. The listed price continued to rise by half a point. There was some divergence in interbank trading, and sentiment was uncertain. In the morning session, Tai Hing, Tai Kang, Run Heng, and Xing Sheng, among others, were buying, while Zhi Feng, Yong Da, De Cheng, Yong Feng, and Fu Chang were mostly selling. The early market declined slightly, likely due to the increase in silver bar prices. Afterwards, there were sudden ups and downs, with the price once falling to around 561 taels. This was mainly due to active selling. At noon, major players made large purchases, causing the price to rise by two or three taels. In the afternoon, Yong Feng, Shun Li, and others were selling, while there were few buyers. The situation was relatively stable, with only one tael of fluctuation, hovering around 64 taels. The final price was 64 taels. The overall market situation is recorded below.

▲ Slight Changes in the Morning Session: The November opening price was 562 taels and 5 mace, immediately falling by 1 tael and 4 mace. However, the gross trading reached about 3 taels before and after, and large bars had already risen by one-eighth. The silver price was stagnant due to the holiday shutdown. Afterwards, there were fluctuations of about one tael, from 63 taels 2 or 3 mace to 1 tael 6 or 7 mace. Then, Heng Xing and Sheng Da bought in, raising the price by 2 taels, to 63 taels 8 mace. The exchange rate for British gold this month among banks was 7 pence 5625, probably because the telegraphic transfer rate announced at 9:30 rose by 125, the US dollar increased by 2.5 jiao, and the Japanese gold price decreased by a small fraction, at 3 taels and 2 mace. However, the internal market was still stable. Zheng Jin bought this month's British telegraphic transfer at 7 pence 5625, so it immediately rose back to 5 or 6 mace, then to 3 taels and 8 mace. Later, the November British gold could be settled at 625. Yong Feng, Yuan Xing, Yong Zhi Feng, Yong Da, De Cheng, and others tended to sell, so the price fell by 3 taels, to 60 taels and 9 qian at 10:30. But in an instant, it immediately rose upwards, because Zhi Feng, Yong Tai, and others started to buy. HSBC also took long-term British gold at 6875, and Zheng Jin also bought January at the same price, so the price was pulled up by more than 1 tael. After 11 o'clock, Heng Xing, Tai Kang, Run Yong Kang, and others suddenly chased after, continuing to rise by more than 1 tael, reaching 63 taels and 8 mace, with only slight fluctuations of 2 or 3 qian. The noon closing price was 63 taels and 7 qian, then it rose again to 4 taels, mainly due to arbitrageurs constantly buying. The telegraphic transfer rate was changed to 610 taels and 2 qian because the Japanese gold price was listed at a small fraction, at 46 or 47 taels to 49 taels, and at 47 taels within the noon hour.

▲ The Afternoon Market Was Neither Good Nor Bad: The afternoon market opened at 63 taels 9 qian, then to 4 taels. Yong Feng, Yuan Mao Yong, and others came to sell, so it fell back to 63 taels 2 qian. Afterwards, Sumitomo and HSBC mutually traded December British gold at 7 pence 625. MacKay also bought in, and there seemed to be more buyers in the market, so it increased by 1 tael. Around 3 o'clock, it was 64 taels and 4 qian, then it decreased by a small 7 or 8 qian. At 4 o'clock, arbitrage houses made some purchases, so it rose to 64 taels 5 qian, and then there were slight advances and retreats of a few qian. The exchange rate was flat, and sentiment was not bad. The closing price at 4:30 was 64 taels, only increasing by 1 qian compared to the day before. However, the falling trend of many days has begun to subside. The highest price of the day was 64 and a half taels, and the lowest price was 60 taels and 9 qian, with a difference of 3 taels and 6 qian. The telegraphic transfer rate was still quoted at 45 or 46 taels. The logged prices were 68 taels to 64 taels, and the margin call was 68 taels. The goods opened at 2 and a half taels in the morning, closed at 4 taels at noon, 3 taels and 9 qian in the afternoon, and closed at 4 taels and 2 qian.

▲ Seemingly Inconsistent Inflows and Outflows: There were many transactions among the various firms. Tai Xing, Sheng Da, Tai Kang Run, Yong Kang, Yuan Tai, Yuan Mao, Jin An, and Yu Xing Yong all bought in. Zhi Feng Yong, Yuan Cheng Yong, Yuan Xing Yong, Shun Li, Da De Cheng, Wan Xing, Yong Feng, Yuan Mao Yong, and Shun Li all sold. Fu Chang, Da De Cheng, and retail investors all bought in. However, the transactions of the various firms were not as strong as in the morning session. The Ningbo (Dalian) group still sold, totaling one thousand several hundred bars, with inflows of five or six hundred bars. The Guangdong group bought a total of one thousand four or five hundred bars, and speculators covered their short positions. According to people in the industry, the long side will still be paying four or five taels for this swap.

Foreign Exchange: Both Official and Unofficial Rates Easing 161

Yesterday, the overseas silver market saw further easing. However, due to the US holiday, the market was mediocre. Zhejiang Province Autumn Cocoons Inventory Will Be Cleared 174

This year's autumn cocoon harvest in various prefectures of Zhejiang Province was poor. Most of the bulk has already been shipped to Shanghai. There are still a small number of dried cocoons stored in various railway station warehouses, waiting for the railway bureau to allocate vehicles for loading and transportation. Rice Market 187

South Shanghai

Yesterday, the rice market in South Shanghai saw approximately 15 or 16 incoming boats. Sales on this street were relatively active, with white japonica rice prices rising by 2 or 3 jiao. The prices of other varieties remained stable.

Shanghai Market

Business News 196

▲The Fair Steel Factory, located west of Wangping Street on Nanjing Road, announces: Due to the official opening of our factory, we are now in a discount period. We manufacture a large variety of steel furniture, all of which is extremely exquisite. Among them, the Fair [stool] is the most practical and popular with the public. Made entirely of pure steel, it is extremely sturdy and durable. The design is both lightweight and convenient, the paint color is smooth and beautiful, and the selling price is extremely low. Normally, each stool sells for one dollar and fifty cents, but during the discount period, there is a 10% discount on all purchases. For home use, it is both beautiful and economical. To increase customer interest and expand their benefits, our factory is sacrificing ten thousand dollars. For every Fair stool purchased, there is a chance to win fifteen hundred dollars. Therefore, since the discount began, the total number of Fair stools sold each day has been over a thousand, and the number of large-scale orders is also very large, etc.

▲The Sino-French Clock and Watch Store announces: Our store is located at the intersection of Avenue Dubail and West Zilaihuo Street. We have strong capital and a large scale. In addition to clocks and watches and eyeglasses, we also sell phonographs and records. We have also recruited experienced repair technicians with superb skills and expertise to provide repair services to customers at low prices. We have now completed renovations and will be opening soon. All goods are very cheap, especially the gold-plated rectangular watches, which are the cheapest. The price is only a few dollars each, but due to cost considerations, the offer is limited to five hundred watches. Purchasers should act quickly to avoid disappointment, etc.

▲The Jianshe Bookstore on Belle Road announces: Our bookstore believes that toys are related to children's education, so we have independently manufactured various types of domestic toys, divided into wood, cloth, and clay, etc. Since their launch, they have been well-received by both Chinese and Westerners.
